## [v4.65.0] — 2026-07-06 — feat(dispatch): Layer A — departments-that-use-skills (task → skill matcher)

The CEO now hands the doer the installed CAPABILITIES most relevant to a task, not just a specialist + SOP. `matchSkillsForTask()` (in `src/lib/context-pack.ts`) globs the box's installed `SKILL.md` files, dept-scopes the candidates via the onboarding `skill-department-map.json`, scores the task text against each skill, and returns the top-3 — which are rendered into the dispatch message as a **"SKILLS AVAILABLE FOR THIS TASK"** block so the specialist reaches for the right playbook instead of reinventing a capability it already has. Wired into BOTH dispatch paths (auto + manual). Repo is fleet-wide — no client names, chat IDs, operator paths, or secrets in any changed file; no Anthropic model ids in any client-facing path. `tsc --noEmit` clean; full vitest CI suite green (95); new node:test suite green (8); qc-cc.sh PASS (111 green). All 5 version locations agree at v4.65.0; annotated tag cut before PR.

- **Skill matcher reuses the department-router's own machinery (no second embedding stack).** Scoring goes through the SAME `getEmbeddingApiKey()` / `fetchEmbeddings()` / `cosineSimilarity()` used by `department-router.ts`: when the CLIENT'S OWN embedding key is configured, each skill's `name. description` is embedded alongside the task text and ranked by cosine, keeping only matches at/above a `SKILL_MATCH_FLOOR` (default 0.55, env-overridable). With no key — or on any API error, or when nothing clears the floor — it falls back to keyword-overlap scoring (reusing the pack's `keywordsFromTask`), so the feature works with zero configuration. Client sovereignty preserved: the client's own key, never a shared/operator one.
- **Dept-scoped candidates via the onboarding `skill-department-map.json` (resolved on-box, env-overridable).** The map is resolved through the per-platform onboarding locations (or pinned with `SKILL_DEPARTMENT_MAP` / `CC_SKILL_DEPARTMENT_MAP`) and normalized from any of three shapes — `{departments:{dept:[skills]}}`, `{skills:{skill:[depts]}}`, or a bare `{skill:[depts]}` — to `skill → canonical-dept-slug[]` (via `canonicalDeptSlug`). Scoping rules: a skill mapped to another department is excluded for the routed dept; an UNMAPPED skill is globally available; a skill mapped to a global token (`*`/`all`/`global`/…) is available to every department; a task with no department sees all skills.
- **Skill roots are env-overridable and symlink-aware.** `SKILL_SEARCH_ROOTS` / `CC_SKILL_ROOTS` pin the exact roots (test/CI determinism); otherwise the common on-box skill install locations + the onboarding-shipped skills tree are probed per-platform. The `SKILL.md` walk is depth- and count-capped (never hangs dispatch on a misconfigured root) and stat-follows symlinked skill directories — plugin skills under `~/.claude/skills` are frequently symlinks, whose `Dirent` reports neither file nor dir, and would otherwise be silently missed.
- **Never throws on the dispatch hot path.** `matchSkillsForTask()` degrades to `[]` on ANY failure (documented contract); both dispatch call sites additionally wrap the call so a skill-match failure can never block a dispatch. `ContextPack` gains a `matched_skills: MatchedSkill[]` field (defaults to `[]`, never undefined) and a new `'skill'` `DocPointerKind`; `renderContextPackSection()` renders the block via the shared `renderMatchedSkillsSection()` helper so the manual route — which does not build a full pack — renders it identically.
- **Auto path (`src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts` → `autoDispatchTask`)** computes the matches (async, before the synchronous pack builder) and threads them into `buildContextPack({ …, matchedSkills })`. **Manual route (`src/app/api/tasks/[id]/dispatch/route.ts`)** computes the matches and splices `renderMatchedSkillsSection()` into the task message for operator-clicked-dispatch parity.
- **Tests (`tests/unit/departments-use-skills-layer-a.test.ts`, node:test):** globbing + keyword ranking (most-relevant skill first, unrelated skills excluded), top-3 cap + explicit `limit`, dept-scoping (mapped-elsewhere skill excluded / included for its own dept / unmapped skill global), symlinked-skill discovery, empty-roots → `[]`, the "SKILLS AVAILABLE FOR THIS TASK" render, and `buildContextPack` threading `matched_skills` through to the render. No network — every embedding-provider key is cleared so the keyword path is deterministic.
- **Independent QC (clean-code-guard skill):** reviewed for correctness / robustness / clean-code. No high or critical findings; the one low-severity real-world coverage gap (symlinked skill dirs skipped by `Dirent` type checks) was fixed and covered by a test. Independent QC score: 9.0/10 — PASS.

## [v4.64.0] — 2026-07-06 — feat(interview): AI Workforce Interview overhaul — bulletproof pause/resume continuity, known-context memory, 3 contract-bug fixes, question-set upgrade, design-system unification (July-3rd-app hardening)

MASSIVE improvement pass over the `/interview` surface (the AI Workforce Interview app that gates Command-Center provisioning, built in the July-3rd update). Locate→analyze→fix→verify: three CONTRACT BUGS that broke core flows in production were found and fixed, pause/resume continuity is now server-derived and exact, the interview remembers what it already knows (confirm-or-correct with real provenance), the structured question set gained a designed-but-never-wired operations section, and the last off-design screen was folded onto the shared design system. Every canonical-write doctrine is preserved: files stay the single source of truth, all writes still go exclusively through the Skill-23 scripts, no new trigger paths, no Anthropic models, no client names. Fresh live verification end-to-end (structured flow → refresh-resume → skip/circle-back → department board 28/28 → provenanced yes/no decisions → triple-gated complete → locked-shell unlock → mobile 390px no-overflow).

- **BUG FIX 1 (P0) — every structured card submit 400'd.** The cards posted `{questionId, storeOn, kind, value}` while `/api/interview/answer` required `{answer, prompt?, …}` — schema validation failed on EVERY structured answer ("Something went wrong saving that"). All cards now build their body through ONE shared builder (`src/lib/interview/answer-payload.ts`), the route's schema moved to `src/lib/interview/answer-schema.ts` (now `.strict()`), and `tests/unit/interview-answer-contract.test.ts` parses the builder's output with the route's OWN schema for every question — client/route drift now fails CI instead of failing owners.
- **BUG FIX 2 — the "Build my company" button died whenever a chat session existed.** ReviewScreen POSTed `{sessionId}` to `/api/interview/complete`, whose `.strict()` schema rejects unknown keys → 400 on the one button the whole interview leads to. The trigger now sends the empty body the route expects.
- **BUG FIX 3 — logo file-drop never worked.** LogoDropCard produces `data:image/*` URLs (≤2MB), but the route rejected everything non-http(s) AND capped answers at 20k chars. The route now accepts bounded inline images: the FULL data URL mirrors onto `clients.logo_url` (BrandTheme renders it) while the transcript records a short human line ("Uploaded a logo file (image/png, ~240 KB)…") instead of a megabyte of base64.
- **CONTINUITY — resume is exact, server-derived, and survives everything.** New pure module `src/lib/interview/structured-progress.ts`: `/api/interview/state` matches transcript Q/A blocks against the question set (same normalization as the answers route) and reports `structured.{answeredIds, nextIndex, complete}`. The client reconciles from that server truth, so a refresh / new browser / Telegram hop lands on the FIRST unanswered card — never consent, never question 1, never a duplicate transcript block (previously `structIndex` was client-only state: a refresh restarted the deck or dumped the owner into the conversation with cards unfinished). WelcomeBack shows the exact next question in its own words. The gateway conversation session id persists per interview (localStorage keyed by the seam's stable `interviewSessionId`, which `/state` now exposes read-only) so a reload continues the SAME interviewer session. Structured skips persist per device and surface as circle-back chips that re-open the exact card.
- **MEMORY — the interview uses what it already knows.** `/state` exposes `knownContext` (client record + company settings, placeholder values filtered): the matching card prefills the fact and offers "Confirm & continue" — an unchanged confirm posts `confirmedFromContext`, recorded as the `confirmed-from-context: <source>` provenance QC check #5 expects (the API supported this; nothing used it). Later prompts personalize with the company name on screen ("What feeling do you want the Verify Labs brand to evoke?") while the CANONICAL prompt is always what's recorded, so matching/QC stay exact (possessive-aware replacement). The conversation kickoff/resume turns brief the interviewer with the owner's name + a don't-re-ask instruction.
- **DEAD-END FIX — a slow interviewer reply no longer forces a resend.** `/api/interview/turn` gains a read-only GET (`?sessionId&after`) and the client polls it for up to 90s after a `pending` turn, delivering the reply when it lands. A progress-stamp failure after a successful transcript append (`appended:true` on 502/503) is now a SOFT success — the owner advances (the answer IS saved) instead of being stuck on an un-fixable card.
- **QUESTIONS — better set, zero duplication.** Identity + operations questions now live in ONE client-safe module (`src/lib/interview/base-questions.ts`) imported by both the Node question set and the client (they were hand-duplicated, drift-prone). company_name gains help copy (brand vs legal name); industry's help explains WHY it's asked (drives department recommendations; specific beats generic). NEW `command_center_name` question completes the pre-plumbed `operations` section (labels/milestones existed with zero questions): optional, jargon-free ("your company's home base"), fills `company.commandCenterName` — previously only settable by an operator post-closeout. Branding stays vendored/canonical (sync test untouched, PASS).
- **SYSTEM CONNECTION — interview answers now land where the unlocked dashboard reads.** `client.name` answers mirror onto the clients row + `companyName` in company-config; `company.industry` / `company.commandCenterName` mirror into `config/company-config.json` via a new atomic-merge helper (`src/lib/interview/company-mirror.ts`, same allow-list as the Settings route). Best-effort/files-win: a mirror failure never unwinds a canonical write. Progress stamps now actually advance during the structured phase (cards send `questionNumber` + `phase`; previously nothing was stamped, so the rail sat at 0%).
- **UI/UX — one design system, honest states, accessible.** WelcomeBack restyled from its hardcoded slate/indigo palette onto the shared `iv-*` tokens (it now re-themes to the client's brand like every other screen) and gained next-up prompt + structured circle-back chips. ProgressRail: server-derived percent (one formula, one place), live "N answers saved" truth line + a "Saved just now ✓" flash on every save (aria-live), semantic `<ol>` steps with `aria-current`, real `progressbar` semantics. ConversationPane announces interviewer turns (aria-live). `MotionConfig reducedMotion="user"` respects OS reduced-motion across all interview animation. Consent screen: picking "What happens with my answers?" relabels Begin ("I'm ready — begin interview") so learning isn't a dead end, plus a "Checking for saved progress…" boot line. New `.iv-known-note` / `.iv-chip` tokens ride the brand variables.
- **Tests:** +16 unit tests across 2 new suites (contract pinning incl. legacy-shape rejection + oversize/inline-logo bounds; resume math incl. mid-deck pause, non-contiguous answers, skip interaction, personalization canonicality). Full suite: 581 tests, zero new failures (the 8 pre-existing failures on main are outside the interview surface). `tsc --noEmit` clean, `next build` clean, interview-jargon lint PASS (17 files), branding sync-test PASS.
- **Fresh live verification (sandboxed HOME + real Skill-23 scripts v17.0.17):** structured answers append byte-shaped transcript blocks + stamp state (`lastQuestionNumber` advances, `interviewSessionId` minted); refresh mid-deck → WelcomeBack "4 answers saved" → resumes at the exact next card; skip → chip → circle-back re-opens the exact card; conversation degrades gracefully with the gateway down and the transcript gate still unlocks departments; board renders the LIVE 28-dept floor, YES/NO land as fully-provenanced decision objects via `record-dept-decision.sh`; review lists every answer; complete pre-flight + `update-interview-state.sh --complete` → `interviewComplete=true`, QC pending → calm needs-review (never a false pass); locked shell verified both ways (/ → 302 /interview before; dashboard unlocks after); 390px mobile: no horizontal overflow.

## [v4.63.0] — 2026-07-06 — feat(dashboard): full UX/design + kanban + settings + models + health-rating + responsive improvement pass

A cross-cutting improvement pass across the whole Command Center dashboard: a cohesive design/nav system with real mobile navigation, a kanban board whose drag/move/CRUD actually persist (Blocked is finally reachable, errors surface instead of silently snapping back), honest settings + a fixed models engine (the Ollama-Cloud cascade now actually selects; operator model overrides now win), a truthful company/department health-rating (no fabricated 72s / hardcoded B grades), and verified responsive layout at mobile/tablet/desktop. Repo is fleet-wide — no client names, chat IDs, GHL location IDs, operator paths, or secrets in any changed file; box user, not root. No new npm dependencies; no Anthropic model ids introduced into any client-facing path (one hardcoded Anthropic id was REMOVED from the Header model list). All 5 version locations agree at v4.63.0; annotated tag cut.

### Structural / data-layer
- **Fresh-DB seed no longer crashes (`src/lib/db/seed.ts`, `src/lib/db/schema.ts`, `scripts/demo-seed.js`).** A brand-new database failed to seed at all: `agents.workspace_id` defaults to `'default'` with a FK to `workspaces(id)`, but nothing seeded that structural row, so the Orchestrator INSERT threw `SQLITE_CONSTRAINT_FOREIGNKEY`. The seed now guarantees the structural `'default'` workspace first (idempotent, carries no client/demo content). The base `tasks.status` CHECK in `schema.ts` was widened to the 10-status board model (`backlog, inbox, planning, pending_dispatch, assigned, in_progress, review, testing, blocked, done`) so a fresh DB is born in lockstep with `TaskStatus`/`validation.ts` (migration 076 already anticipated this and skips when the widened CHECK is present). `demo-seed.js` used invalid priority literals (`normal`/`urgent`) that fail the priority CHECK — corrected to `medium`/`critical`.

### Kanban board (features that actually work)
- **Drag/move errors now surface + revert (`src/components/MissionQueue.tsx`, new `src/components/kanban/BoardToast.tsx`).** A failed status change previously left the optimistic move in place (desync) or silently snapped back. All non-ok responses now revert the move AND raise a dismissible toast with the server's actual reason; the existing "Triad incomplete" 400 still opens the edit modal so the user can fix the missing description/SOP/persona.
- **Blocked is finally reachable (new `src/components/kanban/BlockTaskModal.tsx`).** Dropping/moving a card to Blocked used to 400 every time (the API requires `blocked_reason` ∈ {decision,approval,credential,payment}, `blocked_on_human` ∈ {owner,operator}, and a non-empty `ask`). Moving to Blocked now opens a modal collecting those three fields and PATCHes them; cancel reverts. Verified end-to-end: an in-progress task moved to Blocked persists `status=blocked, blocked_reason, blocked_on_human, ask`.
- **Touch-friendly moves (new `src/components/kanban/MoveTaskMenu.tsx`).** Native HTML5 drag-and-drop does not work on touch, so every card gets an accessible "Move task" menu (real button + `role=menu`) that runs the same status-change path (including the Blocked modal) — the board is now usable on phones/tablets.
- **Real-time deletes (`src/lib/store.ts`, `src/hooks/useSSE.ts`).** The DELETE route already broadcast `task_deleted`, but the store/SSE had no handler — deleted cards lingered. Added `removeTask(id)` + a `task_deleted` SSE case.
- **DELETE 500 fixed (`src/app/api/tasks/[id]/route.ts`).** Deleting any task that had persona-selection/performance history threw a generic 500: `persona_selection_log` and `persona_performance` carry a plain (no-action) NOT-NULL FK to `tasks(id)`, hard-blocking the delete under `foreign_keys=ON`. The handler now clears those task-scoped analytics rows first. Verified: delete now returns `{success:true}`.
- **Create-as-blocked rejected (`src/app/api/tasks/route.ts`).** A brand-new task could be POSTed with `status:blocked`, silently dropping the (uncarried) blocked fields — a card parked in Blocked with no reason. Create-as-blocked now returns a descriptive 400 pointing at the correct flow; the Blocked column's "+" create button is hidden (you reach Blocked by moving an in-flight task).
- **Per-column create + wider status set + search + empty states.** The column "+" seeds the new task's status from that column; the create modal's status dropdown is widened to the real board statuses with human labels; a clearable board search filters by title/description; the no-op "By Status" filter chip (identical to "By Total Tasks") was removed; empty columns show a muted "No tasks" hint.
- **`/tasks/all` resilience (`src/app/tasks/all/page.tsx`).** Added a 60s task refetch so the cross-department board doesn't go stale when SSE is blocked.
- **UI-created tasks keep their department (`src/lib/tasks.ts`).** `createTaskCore` now backfills `department` from the workspace slug when omitted, so UI-created tasks no longer vanish under the `/tasks/all` department filter.

### Settings (honest + persistent)
- **Intelligence Settings clear + lock surfacing (`src/app/api/settings/intelligence/route.ts`, `src/app/settings/intelligence/page.tsx`).** You can now CLEAR a saved model/persona override (a `null`/`''` value deletes the row, respecting the lock check) via a "Reset to inherited" affordance; a locked-setting 423 now names the lock holder + reason instead of a generic "Failed to save".
- **Provider status is honest (`src/components/settings/IntelligenceProviderList.tsx`, `src/app/api/models/provider-status/route.ts`).** The badge that only means "a key string exists somewhere" now reads "Key present" (not "Configured") with a note that presence ≠ verified.
- **Settings hub de-lied (`src/app/settings/page.tsx`, `src/lib/config.ts`).** The page persisted path/URL fields to localStorage that the server never reads (and a `defaultProjectName` field nothing consumes). The dead field is removed; the path/URL values are shown as a read-only "server uses environment variables" reference; the page is a clean hub linking Company + Intelligence settings.
- **Company Settings reflects + reports truthfully (`src/lib/company-config.ts`, `src/components/CompanySettingsForm.tsx`, `src/app/settings/company/page.tsx`).** Brand colors/logo are now read back so the form shows persisted state, and a failed/absent live-branding apply shows a visible "Saved to config, but live branding not applied: <reason>" warning instead of a silent "Saved!".

### Models engine (wiring that applies)
- **Ollama-Cloud cascade actually selects (`src/lib/model-selector.ts`).** `tierOf()` only classified Tier 1 for `ollama/<model>:cloud`, but the Ollama-Cloud connector emits `ollama-cloud/<model>` — so Ollama Cloud fell to Tier 3 (free-only) and the advertised "Ollama Cloud → OpenRouter OSS → Free" cascade never selected it. `tierOf()` now recognizes `ollama-cloud/` (Tier 1) and `ollama-local/` alongside the legacy shape; the docstring is truthful.
- **Operator model overrides now win (`src/lib/intelligence-resolver.ts`).** The role-level and department-level overrides an operator sets in Intelligence Settings were resolved BELOW the auto-selector, so they almost never applied despite the UI claiming authority. The resolution order now places role override and dept default ABOVE the auto-selector (task pin → SOP pin → role override → dept default → auto-selector → sovereign default), still passing explicit picks through the sovereignty/forbidden-model gate (a forbidden explicit pick is skipped with a logged reason).
- **Header model list is dynamic (`src/components/Header.tsx`).** The hardcoded `MODEL_OPTIONS` (which included an `anthropic/…` id and drifted from reality) is replaced with a list loaded from the intelligence API; the Anthropic id is gone.

### Company / department health-rating (truthful scoring)
- **No fabricated scores (`src/components/ceo-board/redesign/DepartmentPulseStrip.tsx`, `src/lib/routing/resolve-department.ts`, `src/components/CEODashboard.tsx`).** The pulse strip fabricated a `72` for empty/low-activity departments; `resolve-department` hardcoded `grade:'B', gradeScore:75` for every department; the CEO dashboard used a headcount-dominated bogus formula. All three now use the real `computeDepartmentGrade`/`computeCompanyHealth` from `src/lib/grading.ts` (honest null-gating on insufficient samples) and render "—"/"Insufficient data" instead of a color-coded lie when there isn't enough data.
- **Honest counts + trends (`src/components/ceo-board/redesign/CompanyHeroCard.tsx`, `KPIStatCards.tsx`).** Active-agent counts now match the real `agents.status` enum (`working`), and the hardcoded "Increased from last week" trend is replaced with a real week-over-week comparison from `/api/performance` (or no trend label when there's no history); velocity is clearly labeled ("per week, 30d avg").

### Design system, navigation, responsive
- **Real mobile navigation (new `src/components/MobileNav.tsx`, `src/app/layout.tsx`).** The retired AppShell left the app with NO mobile nav. A fixed bottom nav (Home/Tasks/Board/Operator/Settings, `md:hidden`, safe-area padding) is mounted app-wide and hidden on the gated `/interview` + `/onboarding` shells; the body gets bottom padding so content is never covered.
- **App-wide command palette (`src/components/CommandPalette.tsx`).** Cmd+K previously listed only the 11 operator sub-routes; it now has a "Navigate" group with every top-level route (including the previously orphaned `/personas` and `/sops`).
- **CEO board header fixed + responsive (`src/app/ceo-board/page.tsx`).** The "Agents" tab pointed at a non-existent `/agent-roster` (404) — repointed to the on-page roster; the header's hardcoded hex colors are tokenized and it no longer overflows on small screens (tabs collapse to a scrollable pill row; non-essential right-cluster items hide below `sm`).
- **Accessible + AA contrast (`src/app/globals.css`, `tailwind.config.ts`, `src/components/Header.tsx`).** `--bcc-text-muted` retoned from `#9CA3AF` (fails WCAG AA on white) to `#6B7280`; icon-only buttons gained aria-labels and focus rings; page backgrounds use the `bcc-bg` token instead of scattered `bg-[#F8F9FB]` literals.
- **Responsive verified at three breakpoints** (Playwright, live): mobile 375px, tablet 768px, desktop 1440px — no horizontal page overflow on Home, Tasks board, CEO board, Intelligence Settings, or Settings; the board scrolls inside its own region; the mobile nav appears at 375, is hidden at ≥768 (top nav takes over).

### Verification
- `npx tsc --noEmit`: 0 errors (clean baseline preserved). `scripts/qc-cc.sh`: PASS (111 green, 4 environmental warnings). `npm run test:unit`: green. Live-verified against a running dev instance: Blocked-move persistence, DELETE now 200, create-as-blocked 400, "Key present" label, honest health "—" states, mobile nav + no-overflow at all three breakpoints.

- **FIX-RESCUE-06 — Path-A outages POST tickets, deterministic id, auto-resolve fixed (`lib/rescue-outage-ticket.sh`).** `heartbeat.sh` / `remediate.sh` now emit one POST per DOWN row: every row → `{action:escalate}` with a deterministic `ticketId` `<client>-<class>-<YYYY-MM-DD>`; a FIXED row → `{action:answer, statusPrefix:"fixed:"}`; an UNFIXED row stays OPEN under SLA. JSON is built by node via env (nothing in the process list); the auth header is read from the secret store and NEVER printed. 22 shell assertions, `bash -n` clean.

## [v4.62.4] — 2026-07-05 — fix(rescue): Rescue Rangers Wave-0 hardening train — 6 fixes (Skills-Analysis-Master-Plan)

Wave-0 hardening of the Rescue Rangers fleet-recovery path (`fleet-heartbeat/`), landing six independent fixes from the Skills-Analysis Master Fix-Plan. All new code is pure/deterministic and lives OUTSIDE the running dashboard, so nothing here touches the Command Center app runtime. Fleet-wide repo hygiene: no client names, chat IDs, GHL location IDs, operator paths, or secrets in any changed file — client/box/person identifiers are always runtime inputs; the durable ticket DB and the return-verify ledger are git-ignored. Tests: 50 `node:test` cases (tier-router 10, ticket-store 12, return-verifier 25, integration 3) + 18 shell assertions (incidents index) all green; every added shell script passes `bash -n`.

- **FIX-RESCUE-02 — watchdog alarm restore + crash-loop detector (`rescue-receiver-watchdog.sh`).** The receiver watchdog's alarm path was dead (`BOT_TOKEN` hardcoded to `""`) — a down receiver was kickstarted forever in silence. The token is re-armed from the secret store (never printed); a first-detection alarm fires once per down-episode, and a bounded auto-restart budget (`MAX_RESTARTS=5`) now distinguishes a transient stall from a genuine CRASH-LOOP: once the budget is exhausted while still down, kickstarting STOPS and a distinct crash-loop escalation pages the operator to check `rescue-receiver-run.sh` / `.env`. Both alarms are flag-file deduped and re-arm only on a 200 (down→up). Hard `ulimit` CPU/mem caps, no loops, all curl calls `--max-time` bounded. The alarm destination (`FIXER_GROUP_CHAT_ID` / `FIXER_THREAD_ID`) and bot token are loaded from the secret store — never hardcoded — and the path degrades gracefully when unset.
- **FIX-RESCUE-05 — real MEDIUM tier + per-tier walls + queue-cap-above-agent-wall (`lib/rescue-tier-router.mjs`).** Routing defaulted the MOST COMMON tickets (coach-client-agent / how-to) to `tier:"hard"` → `kimi-k2.6:cloud@high`, blowing both the ~570s agent wall and the 600s queue cap and paging a human (live evidence: a ticket abandoned at 602.2s). New MEDIUM tier routes coach/how-to → `deepseek-v4-flash:cloud@low` with a ~210s wall; per-tier agent walls for the light-model tiers; and `deriveQueueTimeout` derives the per-job queue cap to sit STRICTLY ABOVE the tier's agent wall so the agent's own graceful timeout fires first (the brutal queue hard-cap no longer pre-empts it). Extracted as a standalone pure module so it is unit-testable WITHOUT importing the receiver (which carries the client return-leg allowlist). All tiers Ollama-Cloud only (binding 2026-07-01).
- **FIX-RESCUE-07 — durable ticket store, RR- numbers, state machine, SLA auto-escalation (`lib/rescue-ticket-store.mjs`, `rescue-sla-sweep.mjs`, `rescue-report.mjs`, `lib/rescue-receiver-store-hook.mjs`).** The live store was n8n workflow static data — WIPED on every workflow re-import, never GC'd, no durable ids/ownership/SLA/audit. Replaced with a single `node:sqlite` (DatabaseSync, Node ≥ 22.5) WAL database on the operator filesystem OUTSIDE n8n: full schema, monotonic human-facing `RR-000123` numbers, a validated state machine (OPEN→ACK→IN_PROGRESS→{RESOLVED|ESCALATED|NEEDS_HUMAN}→CLOSED + REOPENED) with a `ticket_events` audit trail, ownership, severity-derived SLAs with an auto-escalation sweep, a read view, and a GC pass. FAILS CLOSED (throws a clear error if `node:sqlite` is unavailable rather than dropping tickets); illegal transitions throw; all SQL is parameterized. DB path git-ignored.
- **FIX-RESCUE-09 — verify + gate the VPS return leg behind a per-box smoke test (`lib/rescue-return-verifier.mjs`).** The VPS return-leg (docker-exec back into a client box) delivered blind. A per-box loopback smoke test now records a `verified:true` ledger entry; `isReturnDeliveryAllowed` GATES the SSH/docker-exec return path on it, and an unverified box falls back to Telegram-group-only delivery — NEVER a blind SSH. Scoped by default to `type:"vps"` docker-exec blast radius (`RESCUE_RETURN_REQUIRE_ALL_VERIFIED` opts every box in). The verify ledger is git-ignored (keys are client box aliases).
- **FIX-RESCUE-10 — change-log monthly rotation + `incidents.tsv` index for pattern_flag (`lib/rescue-incidents-index.sh`).** The Path-B change-log was re-parsed as prose on every hot-path `pattern_flag` lookup (O(n) over an ever-growing file). A compact append-only `incidents.tsv` index makes the lookup a single tiny scan; the change-log rotates monthly (current + previous retained, older archived to `change-log-YYYY-MM.md`), and the index self-heals (rebuilds from the log if empty) and prunes to the retention window. 18 self-test assertions incl. legacy-scanner parity on 36 probes.
- **FIX-RESCUE-12 — archive `.bak`/bridge/remote-rescue out of the deploy path + de-furnace the heartbeat cron (`rescue-12-cleanup.sh`, `fleet-heartbeat-cron.sh`, `ai.openclaw.fleet-heartbeat.plist`, `fleet-heartbeat.crontab`, `.gitignore`).** (i) An idempotent, dry-run-by-default cleanup relocates ~60 dated `*.bak*` files, the retired `rescue-rangers-bridge.py` (a historical secret carrier), and the vestigial `remote-rescue/` repo under a git-ignored `_archive/` (moved with a manifest, never deleted) so the live path is legible and the secret-leak surface shrinks; `.gitignore` hardened so none of it can ever be committed. (ii) The `fleet-heartbeat` OpenClaw cron fired a full LLM agent turn (`sessionTarget:isolated`, a `:cloud` model, `toolsAllow:[exec]`) every fire just to shell the deterministic `heartbeat.sh` — an Ollama-Cloud furnace. Replaced with a direct-command cron (`fleet-heartbeat-cron.sh`) run via launchd plist or system crontab exactly like the poller/watchdog: no agent turn, no model, no tokens; failure tails go to the Rescue Rangers room THROUGH the gateway (`openclaw message send`, never a raw curl), chat id from the `.env` (never hardcoded).
- **Final-QC hardening (this train).** Client-name/operator-path clearance before merge: replaced hardcoded operator homes with the repo's `${CLAWD_HOME:-${HOME}/clawd}` / `${HOME}` convention across the new scripts, templatized the launchd plist with `__HOME__`/`__CLAWD_HOME__` install-time tokens, and moved the watchdog's Fixer-topic destination into the secret store. STRUCTURAL no-client-names scan PASS; box user, not root.

## [v4.62.3] — 2026-07-05 — feat(persona): DEP-5/F3.7+F3.9 — multi-persona decomposition + SOP slots (Command Center side) (Persona-Matching-Overhaul)

Command Center half of findings **F3.7** (wire decomposition end-to-end) and **F3.9** (per-step SOP persona slots). A task that spans multiple crafts is now executed as a DISTINCT best-fit persona per sub-task, and an SOP can declare per-step `persona_slot`s that drive the split. Builds on FDN-3/F4.1 dispatch injection (v4.61.0), FDN-2 no-naked resilience (v4.62.0) and DEP-2/F3.4 SOP-aware matching (v4.62.2); the matcher side (DEP-4, openclaw-onboarding) rolls separately, so the CC path is robust to DEP-4 rollout timing (transparent `--slots` retry, single-persona fallback). Additive + fail-closed; migration 088 is idempotent. Repo is fleet-wide (no client names, chat IDs, or GHL location IDs in any changed file); box user, not root.

- **Migration 088 (`src/lib/db/migrations.ts`).** `task_subtask_persona` = `_SUBTASK_PERSONA_DDL` + `slot` column (F3.9) + `idx` on `task_id`. Additive/idempotent — `CREATE IF NOT EXISTS` for a fresh DB, `ALTER`-adds `slot` onto an older hand-run-CLI-created (slot-less) table.
- **Decision + plan (`src/lib/tasks.ts`).** `decideMultiPersona` picks `--combined` when the resolved SOP declares >1 `persona_slot` OR a FREE heuristic probe (`heuristicDecompose`, a faithful pure-regex TS mirror of `decompose-task.py`) yields >1 sub-task on a NON-mechanical task; else single-persona. `resolvePersonaPlanAndPin` persists plan rows, pins the seq-1 primary onto `tasks.persona_*` for back-compat, and enforces the FDN-1 fallback guarantee on every REQUIRED slot (empty required slot → dept-default persona + `persona_fallback` audit event). Never leaves a task naked — falls back to single selection on failure. The single-persona path stays SOP-aware (DEP-2/F3.4 `sopContext` preserved through the merge).
- **`persona-selector.ts` / dispatch.** `selectPersonaPlanForTask` spawns `decompose-task.py --combined`; `loadSubtaskPersonas` reads the plan (tolerant of pre-088 boxes); `broadcastPersonaPlan` re-emits `task_updated`. Dispatch renders a PERSONA PLAN block — one Section-4 load pointer per non-mechanical sub-task by REUSING the FDN-3 `buildPersonaBlock` ×N — `''` for a single-persona task (no regression). Coexists with FDN-2 `ensurePersonaForDispatch` + DEP-2 `rescorePersonaWithSOP`.
- **SOP slots + kanban card.** `PersonaSlot` step-level contract in `src/lib/sops.ts` (`validatePersonaSlot` / `getPersonaSlots`, durable across SOP-edit routes); `PersonaSlotChips` renders one slot chip per sub-task on a decomposed task.
- **Tests (14, all pass):** `dep5-persona-plan-multi` + `dep5-no-naked-persona-plan`. `tsc --noEmit` clean; FDN-3 dispatch 8/8 green; zero new failures vs baseline.
- **Re-land note (v4.62.3).** Merged `origin/main` (through v4.62.2) into `fix/DEP-5` (merge, not rebase → no force-push). Resolved `tasks.ts`: unioned imports; DEP-5's multi-persona decomposition block and main's DEP-2 rescore + FDN-2 dispatch-gate functions all coexist; the create-time single-persona call keeps F3.4's `sopContext`. All 5 CC version locations agree at v4.62.3; annotated tag cut.

## [v4.62.2] — 2026-07-05 — fix(persona): DEP-2/F3.4-cc — SOP-aware persona matching (Command Center side) (Persona-Matching-Overhaul)

Command Center half of finding **F3.4** — the running SOP now informs the persona match. Builds on the merged FDN-3/F4.1 dispatch injection (v4.61.0) and CONSUMES DEP-1's `--sop-slug` / `--sop-name` / `--sop-hints` selector inputs (matcher side, separate train). Additive at the module level plus a bounded, fail-closed behavioral change to the auto-dispatch builder; no schema migration (`sops.persona_hints` already exists — it had five writers and zero readers until now). Repo is fleet-wide (no client names, chat IDs, or GHL location IDs in any changed file); box user, not root.

- **Creation-time SOP-aware match (`src/lib/tasks.ts`).** `createTaskCore` already runs the SOP auto-suggest BEFORE persona selection; now the winning SOP's `slug` + `name` + parsed `persona_hints` are captured (`sopSelectorContextFromRow` / `loadSopSelectorContextById` / `parsePersonaHints`) and threaded through `resolvePersonaAndPin` → `selectPersonaForTask` to the selector. `persona_hints` parsing is defensive: non-array/malformed JSON → `[]`, and empty/sentinel ids are dropped so a stale hint list can never poison the candidate pool.
- **Dispatch-time RESCORE on SOP change (`src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts`).** Persona selection runs at creation — before we know which SOP will govern the work. When the SOP resolved at dispatch (canonical copy, the `getBestSOPForTask` re-pull, or an operator edit) differs from the one the creation-time selection saw (`task.sop_id` at dispatch entry — most commonly: selection saw NONE and an SOP was resolved here), dispatch re-runs selection WITH the SOP context (`rescorePersonaWithSOP`) and patches the in-memory row so `buildPersonaBlock` DELIVERS the rescored persona in the SAME message. Bounded (single-shot, `PERSONA_RESCORE_TIMEOUT_MS=10s`, no retry loop), and it persists a queryable `persona_rescored_at_dispatch` audit event.
- **NO-NAKED / fail-closed (Skill-23 SOP-07 posture).** The rescore NEVER downgrades a persona the task already carries: a null / mechanical (`no_persona_required`) / sentinel selector result keeps the existing pin untouched — only a concrete, non-sentinel persona replaces it. The whole rescore is non-fatal (dispatch proceeds regardless).
- **Defensive selector glue (`src/lib/persona-selector.ts`).** `selectPersonaForTask` gains optional `sopContext` + bounded-`timeoutMs` params and forwards `--sop-*` flags only when the context carries something usable (`buildSelectorArgv` / `hasSopContext`, exported + unit-tested). On a box whose `persona-selector-v2.py` predates DEP-1, the strict argparse rejects the unknown flags (exit 2 / "unrecognized arguments"); we detect that and retry ONCE without the SOP flags — degrading to a non-SOP-aware match rather than failing the whole task to the department-default fallback. All other failures are NOT swallowed.
- **Contract tests (`tests/unit/dep2-sop-aware-matching.test.ts`, 10 cases):** `--sop-*` forwarding (incl. the multi-persona-hint pool comma-joined), partial-context trimming, defensive `persona_hints` parsing, `sopSelectorContextFromRow` / `loadSopSelectorContextById` from a seeded SOP row, the no-naked never-downgrade invariant (null + mechanical results), and the happy path re-pin + `persona_rescored_at_dispatch` event. `tsc --noEmit` clean; FDN-3 / Point-10 / PRD-1.5 / PRD-1.6 persona suites still green.
- **Re-land note (v4.62.2).** Rebased onto `origin/main` after FDN-2 (v4.62.0) and DEP-11 (v4.62.1) landed. Merge-resolved the `persona-selector.ts` selector-spawn block (kept the DEP-2 `runSelector`/SOP-retry refactor while preserving FDN-2's `PERSONA_SELECT_TIMEOUT_MS`=60s budget) and `tasks.ts` (both the DEP-2 `rescorePersonaWithSOP` and FDN-2 `ensurePersonaForDispatch` functions coexist; imports unioned).

## [v4.62.1] — 2026-07-05 — feat(health): DEP-11/F2.3 — dual-store embedding health on /api/health + fleet heartbeat (Persona-Matching-Overhaul)

Additive observability from the Persona-Matching-Overhaul. Surfaces the TWO parallel embedding stores — the persona index (Gemini-only, `gemini-embedding-2` @3072) and the SOP/routing index (provider-flexible: google @3072 or OpenAI `text-embedding-3-small` @1536) — SIDE BY SIDE on the Command Center health endpoint and in the fleet heartbeat, so an ASYMMETRIC degradation (e.g. an OpenAI-only box that gets semantic SOP routing but keyword-only persona Layer-5) is visible instead of silent. Fully additive: no schema migration, no behavior change to matching or dispatch; the new block never flips the top-level health `status` (keyword fallback still serves — asymmetry is operational, not a downed box). Reads ONLY row metadata (provider/model/dim/counts) — it NEVER reads, resolves, or prints an API key or any secret. Repo is fleet-wide (no client names, chat IDs, or GHL location IDs in any changed file); box user, not root.

- **`shared-utils/embedding_health.py` — the dual-store probe.** A standalone, dependency-free (stdlib `sqlite3`) reader that inspects BOTH stores read-only (`file:…?mode=ro`, 5s busy-timeout) and reports each store's `(provider, model, model_histogram, stale_rows, foreign_provider_rows, semantic_ready, degraded)` plus a top-level `asymmetric` flag + human `asymmetric_detail`. Fail-open / degrade-loudly: it NEVER raises to the caller — a missing DB, missing table, or read error becomes `available:false` + `degraded:true` with a note, not a crash; exit stays 0 unless `--strict` (exit 2 when any store is degraded, for CI/heartbeat gating). Stale = rows on a retired gemini slug (`gemini-embedding-001` retires 2026-07-14); asymmetry fires when one store is semantic-ready and the other keyword-only, OR both are semantic on DIFFERENT providers (split vector space).
- **`src/lib/sop-embeddings.ts` — `getSOPEmbeddingHealth()`.** The TypeScript half / last-resort fallback: reports the SOP store's provider, active model/dims, model histogram, stale count (reused from `countStaleGoogleEmbeddings()` — single source of truth) and semantic-readiness. Never throws; a missing `sop_embeddings` table or DB error returns `available:false` + `degraded:true`.
- **`src/app/api/health/route.ts` — `embeddings` block.** `GET /api/health` gains an additive `embeddings` object computed by spawning `embedding_health.py` (`execFile`, 4s timeout, one retry, `python3 -s`) and passing only the resolved SOP provider NAME (never a key). If python3/the script is unavailable it falls back to the TypeScript SOP snapshot (`source:'ts-fallback'`, persona index reported as indeterminate). The block is additive and its degradation never changes the top-level `status`; the route still returns 200 on error.
- **`scripts/cc-health-check.sh` — heartbeat wiring (NON-GATING WARN).** The fleet heartbeat now runs the probe and logs a one-line side-by-side summary (`persona_index=… | sop_index=…`), emitting `WARN: embedding stores ASYMMETRIC …` when the split is present. It NEVER changes the green/red verdict or exit code (operational, not a correctness fault) and attaches the full JSON to the heartbeat payload under `embedding_health`.
- **Tests.** `shared-utils/test_embedding_health.py` (7 cases — both-healthy/not-asymmetric, OpenAI-only headline asymmetry, split-provider asymmetry, retired-model stale+degraded, missing-DB no-crash, provider-none keyword-only, line-format) and `tests/unit/embedding-health.test.ts` (5 cases — empty/healthy/stale/no-key/provider-mismatch) both green; `tsc --noEmit` clean on the changed TS.

## [v4.62.0] — 2026-07-05 — feat(persona): no-naked-tasks invariant — CC resilience half (F3.1-cc) — Persona-Matching-Overhaul FDN-2

Foundation train FDN-2 of the Persona-Matching-Overhaul. Closes the command-center resilience half of the "naked task" gap: every task now provably carries a persona by dispatch time. Lands ON TOP of FDN-3/F4.1 (v4.61.0), which delivers the matched persona to the doer via the shared `buildPersonaBlock` renderer — FDN-2 guarantees that renderer always has a REAL persona to render instead of the unresolved-governance fallback. Additive + non-breaking; no migration. References `DEFAULT_PERSONA_FALLBACK='blackceo-house-voice'`, registered by FDN-1. Repo is fleet-wide (no client names, chat IDs, or GHL location IDs in any changed file); box user, not root.

- **Selector budget 30s → 60s + pinned fallback constants (`src/lib/persona-selector.ts`).** LLM-mode scoring of ~12 finalists × 4 layers plus a cold embedding call can exceed 30s on a loaded box, turning a slow-but-valid selection into a null result (naked task, path A3). The spawn timeout is raised to `PERSONA_SELECT_TIMEOUT_MS = 60_000` with one retry after 5s. Two pinned constants mirror the Python side: `DEFAULT_PERSONA_FALLBACK = 'blackceo-house-voice'` (the generic, brand-neutral fleet persona — deliberately generic so it never out-scores a specialist, registered by FDN-1) and `GOVERNANCE_PERSONA_FALLBACK = 'covey-7-habits'` (the oversight pointer for mechanical tasks). The selector result now carries `governance_persona_id`.
- **1-retry + TS fallback chain (`src/lib/tasks.ts`).** `PERSONA_PIN_MAX_ATTEMPTS` is now 2 (one real attempt + one retry) before the deterministic fallback engages. `deriveDepartmentDefaultPersona` walks the resolved Q2 chain — **last department `persona_assignment` → `company-config.json` `default_persona_id` → `DEFAULT_PERSONA_FALLBACK` constant** — replacing the old synthetic `dept-default-<slug>` id (whose blueprint did not exist) with a REAL, loadable persona; the selector never returns null. A mechanical `no_persona_required` task stays personaless BY DESIGN but records a `[PERSONA-GOVERNANCE]` oversight pointer (`covey-7-habits` else the per-client override).
- **Synchronous dispatch last-chance gate — heal, not stall (`src/lib/tasks.ts` `ensurePersonaForDispatch`, `src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts`, `src/app/api/tasks/[id]/dispatch/route.ts`).** Both dispatch paths now guarantee a persona at send time: if a task reaches dispatch naked (`settings.persona === 'auto'`), the gate applies the deterministic fallback chain and PINS it to the task row (bounded, no Python on the hot path) — it NEVER holds the task for a persona (availability > purity; the fallback makes NULL impossible). The pinned persona then feeds FDN-3's shared `buildPersonaBlock`, so the doer receives a concrete `**Persona (assigned):**` load contract instead of the unresolved-governance fallback.
- **Persona backfill heal-sweep (`src/lib/jobs/persona-backfill-sweep.ts`, `src/lib/jobs/scheduler.ts`).** Modeled on `backlog-redispatch-sweep.ts`: every 5 minutes, re-runs selection for any aged, non-terminal, persona-less task, retroactively healing A3/A4 and self-healing a box recovering from an empty persona universe (A1). Furnace/loop-proof: exactly one attempt per task ever (guarded by a `persona_backfill_attempt` event), a 120s grace window, and a batch cap. Disable with `PERSONA_BACKFILL_SWEEP_ENABLED=0`.
- **Per-client overrides (`config/company-config.json`).** New nullable `default_persona_id` / `governance_persona_id` fields let an operator pin a client-chosen default/governance persona without a code change; both default to `null` (the pinned constants apply).
- **Contract test (`tests/unit/no-naked-dispatch.test.sh`).** An enforced-invariant test (not hope) drives the real CC code across the A1-A7 persona-less paths via the `PERSONA_FIXTURE_JSON` escape hatch against a throwaway fixture DB, asserting: fallback pin on selector failure, governance pointer on mechanical, dispatch-gate heal, F4.1 pinned-persona delivery, and a global "0 non-mechanical naked tasks" invariant. Wired into qc-cc CI. Companion `point10-persona-exhaustion-fallback.test.ts` updated to the new fallback chain.

## [v4.61.0] — 2026-07-05 — fix(persona): FDN-3/F4.1 — deliver the matched persona to the doer at dispatch (Persona-Matching-Overhaul foundation)

Consolidated release of the Command Center foundation work from the Persona-Matching-Overhaul. Bundles the single merged foundation train on this repo — **FDN-3 / finding F4.1**, the highest-value fix in the persona system — into one repo-version roll (v4.60.1 → v4.61.0). Additive at the module level plus a behavioral change to the two dispatch message builders; no schema migration. Repo is fleet-wide (no client names, chat IDs, or GHL location IDs in any changed file); box user, not root. Independently verified on `origin/main`: both dispatch paths now read `task.persona_id` and deliver the matched persona to the doer.

- **FDN-3 / F4.1 — the matched persona now reaches the executing agent (`src/lib/persona-dispatch.ts`, `src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts`, `src/app/api/tasks/[id]/dispatch/route.ts`).** Both dispatch paths — the fast-loop auto-dispatch (`task-dispatcher.ts`) and the operator-click route (`api/tasks/[id]/dispatch/route.ts`) — previously rendered `settings.persona` and, when it was the string `'auto'`, prose telling the doer to "AUTO-SELECT. Run the 5-Layer Persona Matching Protocol." The persona the selector matched onto the task row (`tasks.persona_id` / `.persona_name` / `.persona_mode`) never reached the doer, so every upstream computation (pipeline, embeddings, 5-layer matching, bonuses, variety, adherence) was discarded at the last hop. A new shared renderer `buildPersonaBlock` (in `persona-dispatch.ts`) is imported by BOTH builders so the two messages are byte-identical for the persona section; it reads `task.persona_id` and emits the same Section-4 (A–D) + §7B load contract that `persona-matching-protocol.md` Step 5 defines — with the id resolved, never self-selected. The AUTO-SELECT / 5-Layer self-selection prose is deleted from both files.
- **`agent_settings.persona` is now an operator LOCK only.** A non-`'auto'` pin via `role_override` / `department_default` hard-overrides the match; `'auto'` now means "defer to the task's matched persona," never "self-select." Task and operator always beat the constant, so client sovereignty is preserved.
- **Never-naked, fail-closed dispatch (Skill-23 SOP-07 posture).** Every branch of `buildPersonaBlock` returns a concrete persona OR an explicit governance oversight pointer — never `'auto'`, never a self-selection protocol, never an empty block. Hybrid tasks render the secondary persona blend; mechanical tasks (`no_persona_required`) carry a governance pointer (`task.governance_persona_id` → `GOVERNANCE_PERSONA_FALLBACK='covey-7-habits'`); unresolved selection falls back to the house governance persona rather than telling the doer to invent one.
- **Contract test (`tests/unit/fdn3-persona-dispatch-injection.test.ts`, 8 cases):** persona-in-message == persona-on-row, Section-4/§7B/[+APPENDIX] present, zero AUTO-SELECT, hybrid secondary, mechanical governance pointer, operator lock, never-naked fallback. `tsc --noEmit` clean. (Landed with the fix in PR #133 @ 1155344.)

## [v4.60.0] — 2026-07-04 — feat(interview): AI Workforce Interview app — the locked /interview surface, seam over the Skill-23 brain, 7-phase flow + triple-gated Build — Big July 3rd Update Wave 5

Wave 5 of The Big July 3rd Update. A new client-facing `/interview` surface that runs the AI Workforce interview (Skill 23 / AI Workforce Blueprint) inside the Command Center, then gates the whole dashboard behind it until closeout. Built by subagents, production-build verified (`npm ci` + `tsc` + `npm run build` all exit 0) and independently verified against a 10-gate integration pass. Additive: the canonical FILES stay the single source of truth — the seam reads them, it never becomes a second write authority. Repo is fleet-wide (no client names, chat IDs, or GHL location IDs in any changed file); box user, not root.

- **Locked `/interview` surface + Edge-safe interview-mode shell lock (`src/middleware.ts`, `src/app/interview/*`, `src/components/interview/InterviewGateSync.tsx`, `src/components/interview/gate-actions.ts`, `src/lib/interview/gate-cookie.ts`).** While the interview is incomplete the middleware 302s every other page route to `/interview`, so the client never lands on an empty dashboard — the full Command Center is the closeout reveal. Edge can't read the DB/filesystem, so a Node server action (`refreshInterviewGate`) derives completion from the two authoritative build-state flags (`interviewComplete` / `buildCompletedAt`) and mints a short-TTL **signed** `mc_interview_complete` cookie that the Edge middleware only READS + verifies. Every non-terminal signal (valid-incomplete, expired-incomplete, absent, forged) **fails CLOSED** to `/interview`; a signature-valid "complete" token is terminal (never reverts). API, `/onboarding`, `/_next`, and asset routes are exempt (no redirect loop).
- **The seam over the Skill-23 brain (`src/lib/interview/seam.ts`, `paths.ts`, `store.ts`, `mirror.ts`).** A pure-fs library that reads the three canonical artifacts — `.workforce-build-state.json`, `workforce-interview-answers.md`, `interview-handoff.md` — and exposes typed readers (`readBuildState` / `readHandoff` / `readInterviewProgress`). The FILES win on every disagreement (same posture as `department-floor.py`); the seam never writes a canonical artifact, never sets `interviewComplete`, never records a decision.
- **6 interview API routes + the answers route (`src/app/api/interview/turn`, `state`, `complete`, `answer`, `decision`, `canonical-departments`, `answers`).** The read/advance surface for the flow: `turn` and `answer` drive the conversational Q/A, `state` returns current phase/progress, `canonical-departments` serves the 25-department canonical set, `decision` records a provenanced department decision, `answers` lists the mirrored Q/A blocks, and `complete` runs the terminal closeout with a pre-flight that mirrors server **gates #2 (transcript) / #3 (coverage) / #8 (declines)** and fails closed with a structured 409 when a gate is unmet.
- **7-phase flow with a triple-gated Build button (`src/components/interview/*`, `src/app/interview/InterviewClient.tsx`).** Consent → structured question cards → conversational pane → progress rail → milestones → department decision board → review. The Build button in the review screen is triple-gated: it honors gate #2 (a real transcript exists), gate #3 (every department has a provenanced decision), and gate #8 (every decline is provenanced) before it will fire — the same three gates the `complete` route enforces server-side (defense in depth).
- **Migration 087 — interview read-mirror (`src/lib/db/migrations.ts`).** New idempotent migration adds `interview_sessions` + `interview_answers`, a **read-mirror / fast-UI index only**. These tables cache what the canonical files already say so the UI renders progress and an answer list without re-parsing on every request; neither is ever a write authority for `interviewComplete` or for the canonical reconciliation decisions. If the mirror and the files disagree, the files win.
- **Jargon lint (`scripts/lint-interview-jargon.ts`, `npm run lint:interview-jargon`).** A lint gate that keeps internal/operator jargon out of the client-facing interview copy.
- **Interview re-engagement nudge worker — DORMANT by default (`src/lib/jobs/interview-nudge-sweep.ts`, `src/lib/jobs/scheduler.ts`).** Re-engages an owner who started the interview and went quiet with a single Telegram message carrying a P0-7-contract resume link. Idempotent (one nudge per session/tier, highest crossed tier only), silent/operator-safe (owner chat only, never the operator, no Live Feed broadcast), and **opt-in**: a no-op unless `INTERVIEW_NUDGE_SWEEP_ENABLED=1` (repo-only until fleet rollout is released; disable entirely with `DISABLE_INTERVIEW_NUDGE_SWEEP=1`).
- **Seam-vs-Python parity harness (`src/lib/interview/__tests__/seam-parity.test.ts`, `__fixtures__/parity/*`, `scripts/seam-parity-golden.py`, `scripts/regen-seam-parity-golden.sh`).** A golden-fixture harness that proves the TypeScript seam readers produce byte-for-byte the same interpretation of the canonical files as the Skill-23 Python side, so the web surface can never drift from the box-side brain.
- **prove-zhe web end-to-end (`tests/e2e/prove-zhe-web.e2e.mjs`, `zhe-web-lib.mjs`, `zhe_gate_probes.py`, `ts-register.mjs`, `ts-resolve-hook.mjs`, `npm run test:prove-zhe-web`).** An e2e proof that drives the locked `/interview` surface through the gate probes end to end.
- **CI wiring (`.github/workflows/qc-cc.yml`).** The QC workflow gains the interview jargon lint + seam-parity + prove-zhe-web checks.

## [v4.59.5] — 2026-07-03 — chore(security): externalize the client roster out of the anti-leak gates (names, chat IDs, GHL location IDs off GitHub) + scrub residual client names — client-name hardening

Security/hardening pass. The real client roster (client names, Telegram chat IDs, GHL location IDs) no longer lives inline in the anti-leak gates — it is externalized to an operator-local, gitignored file and loaded at runtime, so client-identifying data is now 100% off GitHub while the gates still bite (fail-closed) in both modes. All additive; no application logic/routes/schemas changed; repo is fleet-wide; box user, not root.

- **Roster externalized out of the leak gates (`scripts/qc-assert-no-client-names.sh` v2.0.0, `scripts/qc-blocked-gate.sh`).** Both gates previously carried the real client denylist (names + numeric Telegram chat IDs + GHL location IDs) inline in tracked source. That denylist now lives in NO tracked file: it is loaded at runtime from an operator-local, gitignored roster resolved as `$OPENCLAW_CLIENT_ROSTER` → else `~/.openclaw/client-roster.txt`, via a new shared loader `scripts/client-roster-lib.sh`.
- **Two modes, never fail-open.** *Box mode* (roster present — operator box / pre-commit): scans every tracked file (and, for the diff gate, the diff) for every real roster name / chat ID / GHL ID — any hit FAILS (exit 1); this is the authoritative check. *Structural / CI mode* (roster absent, e.g. GitHub Actions without the secret): the gate does NOT silently pass — it still fails closed on the operator machine path and on any leaked obviously-fake `.example` placeholder name, and WARNS that the full roster-specific scan was skipped. Numeric chat-ID hits stay MASKED in output (last 4 digits only).
- **Committed placeholder template + shared loader.** `scripts/client-roster.example.txt` ships as the tracked template — obviously-fake placeholders only, no real data — for operators to copy to `~/.openclaw/client-roster.txt`; `scripts/client-roster-lib.sh` is the sourced loader (path resolution + name / chat-ID / placeholder accessors). `.gitignore` now excludes the repo-local roster copies so a filled-in roster can never be committed.
- **CI wiring (`.github/workflows/qc-cc.yml`).** The `no-client-names` job now (a) runs a hermetic BOX-mode self-test — points the gate at the committed `.example` roster and confirms the planted fixture still fails (exit 1), proving detection bites — then (b) runs the authoritative gate in structural mode against the real tree (operator-path + placeholder-leak scan, fail-closed).
- **Residual client names scrubbed.** Removed the last real client names from a code comment (`src/lib/campaigns.ts`) and a unit-test comment/assertion (`tests/unit/qc-gate-af-spell-spelling-fidelity.test.ts`), and re-based the planted CI fixture (`tests/fixtures/no-client-names/planted-client-name.txt`) onto a placeholder name so the self-test proves the detector without embedding any real name.
- **Result.** Client-identifying data (names, chat IDs, GHL location IDs) is now 100% off GitHub while the leak gates still fail closed in both box and structural/CI mode. Cross-repo consistent with the openclaw-onboarding roster externalization. No client names in any changed file; box user, not root.

## [v4.59.4] — 2026-07-03 — fix(build-status+sync): build-status route scans canonical company roots (#9 consumer), sync-departments no-over-prune (#11), slug-upsert UNIQUE crash (#13) — Big July 3rd Update Wave 3

Wave 3 of The Big July 3rd Update. Built by subagents, independently verified (fresh Opus, PASS on #9 consumer, #11, #13). All additive/idempotent; no client names in any changed file (repo is fleet-wide); box user, not root.

- **#9 (consumer) — build-status route now finds `build-progress.json` without `OPENCLAW_COMPANY_ROOT` exported (`src/app/api/onboarding/build-status/route.ts`).** `findActiveBuildProgress()` previously only scanned `OPENCLAW_COMPANY_ROOT` plus the legacy `/data/.openclaw/workspace/...` layout, so the `/onboarding/building` page showed no progress whenever that env var was not exported in the dashboard's process. It now also scans the canonical ZHC company roots the producer actually writes to — `/data/openclaw-master-files/zero-human-company` (VPS) and `~/Downloads/openclaw-master-files/zero-human-company` (Mac) — kept in sync with the `build-workforce.py` producer's `get_openclaw_paths()` resolution. Pairs with the onboarding **v17.0.12** producer so the building page reflects live build-progress on both platform layouts. No auth/route-shape change; purely an added candidate-root scan.
- **#11 — `sync-departments-from-build-state.py` no longer over-prunes valid rows.** The re-seed widened its existing-set to ALL workspaces (any `company_id`), so rows seeded under a stale `company_id` (e.g. the pre-064 `default`) are now **adopted** (re-homed to the real slug and refreshed) instead of being duplicated or crashing on the `PRIMARY KEY(id)` INSERT. Pruning of stale rows is **opt-in** via a new `--prune` flag (invoked only from `run-full-install` Phase 6c); ad-hoc syncs never delete. When pruning, a `RESERVED_WORKSPACE_IDS` allowlist (infra columns + CEO/master-orchestrator aliases, matched case-insensitively) and a **task-count guard** (any workspace still holding tasks is kept and logged for operator review) prevent deletion of any valid client row.
- **#13 — company upsert no longer crashes on a `UNIQUE(slug)` conflict.** `companies.slug` is UNIQUE, so the previous `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT(id)` raised a UNIQUE(slug) violation whenever an earlier seed had created the company under a different id (e.g. a uuid) with the same slug. The upsert now **queries by slug first** and branches UPDATE/INSERT, making it safe on every SQLite version (no dependency on multi-target `ON CONFLICT`, which needs SQLite ≥ 3.35).
- **Tests.** `tests/unit/test_sync_departments_from_build_state.py` extended to cover the widened existing-set + row adoption/re-homing, the opt-in `--prune` with reserved-allowlist and task-count guards, and the query-by-slug UPDATE/INSERT branch (no UNIQUE(slug) crash). No migration, no schema change.

## [v4.59.3] — 2026-07-03 — fix(seed): stop client-box demo pollution + duplicate master (P0 audit #1) + create sop_feedback table (#5) — Big July 3rd Update Wave 0

Wave 0 of The Big July 3rd Update (functioning-audit fixes). Built by subagents, independently verified (fresh Opus, PASS 5/5).
- **#1 (P0) — demo/duplicate-master pollution:** `seed.ts` now **guards the master Orchestrator insert** (SELECT `is_master=1 'Orchestrator'` first; reuse if present — re-runs can never create a second master) and makes **demo content opt-in** via `DEMO_SEED === 'true'` (default unset = **no demo** on client boxes; `SKIP_DEMO_SEED` removed). `db:push` is now **migrations-only** (new `src/lib/db/migrate.ts` → `getDb()`; no seed); `db:seed` stays the explicit guarded seed. New idempotent migration **086 `remove_demo_seed_rows`** de-dupes masters (keep oldest, FK re-point) and deletes legacy demo agents/tasks/"Team Chat" **only when a real company exists** — all try/catch-guarded, safe to re-run. `.env.example` updated.
- **#5 (P1) — dead SOP feedback loop:** new migration **085 `create_sop_feedback`** creates `sop_feedback(id, sop_id FK→sops, task_id, agent_id, rating INTEGER CHECK IN (1,-1,0), notes, created_at)` + indexes, matching `sop-learning.ts`/`/api/sops/feedback` exactly (revives the thumbs-rating endpoint + learning loop).
