## [v4.59.1] — 2026-07-03 — fix(status-contract): reconcile presentations terminal-status contract (drop orphan 'delivered', single 'done'+cert terminal)

Reconciles an internal contract inconsistency surfaced by the July-3 verification pass. `src/lib/validation.ts` `UpdateTaskSchema` TaskStatus enum has no `'delivered'` (a PATCH carrying it 400s at the schema), yet `src/lib/presentations-cert-gate.ts` listed `'delivered'` as a terminal status — the two files disagreed, so a presentations card could never reach a terminal closed state through the contract. The onboarding presentations rail now closes a completed deck via `status='done'` + a matching `process_certificate_sha` (`'delivered'` is a note, not a status). Fix: removed the orphan `'delivered'` from the cert-gate terminal set (now `{'done'}`); exported `TaskStatus` (values unchanged, 10) + `PRESENTATIONS_TERMINAL_STATUSES` for a new contract test `tests/unit/presentations-cert-contract.test.ts` that pins terminal-statuses ⊆ the schema enum, accepts `done`+valid-cert, and rejects `delivered`. The anti-spoof stored-cert MATCH check is untouched (no gate weakened). Additive/idempotent; no client names (repo is fleet-wide); box user, not root.

## [v4.59.0] — 2026-07-01 — fix(final-review-hardening): persona-exhaustion department-default pin, QC provider-down deferral, backlog-redispatch escalation cap

Closes three board-liveness gaps surfaced during the final review pass. All additive/idempotent; no client names in any changed file (repo is fleet-wide); box user, not root.

- **Persona exhaustion now pins a deterministic department-default (`src/lib/tasks.ts`, migration 083).** `resolvePersonaAndPin()` previously left a task personaless after `PERSONA_PIN_MAX_ATTEMPTS` was exhausted. It now falls back to a deterministic department-default persona and pins it, marking the pin `persona_fallback=1` (new `tasks.persona_fallback` audit column, migration 083, idempotent `ALTER TABLE`) plus a queryable audit event, so the board invariant — every task carries a persona — holds even under total selector exhaustion. A genuinely-matched persona is unaffected; only the exhaustion path sets the flag. `tests/unit/point10-persona-exhaustion-fallback.test.ts` covers the fallback selection, the pin, and the audit flag/event.
- **QC provider-down deferral (`src/lib/qc-scorer.ts`, `src/lib/jobs/qc-review-sweep.ts`).** The heuristic-fallback QC path already distinguished `'no-key'` from `'provider-down'` internally but both landed in ordinary human review. A `'provider-down'` result (a key IS configured but every LLM call failed — outage/network blip) now writes a `[QC-DEFERRED-PROVIDER-DOWN]` marker instead and is held in review rather than surfaced as a human-actionable item; `qc-review-sweep` excludes it from the human-required queue and auto-rescores it on its next pass once the provider recovers, so a transient provider blip can no longer trigger a human-review storm. `'no-key'` (genuinely unconfigured) is unaffected and still routes to normal review. `tests/unit/point6-qc-provider-down-defer.test.ts` covers marker placement, sweep exclusion, and auto-rescore on recovery.
- **Backlog-redispatch escalation cap (`src/lib/jobs/backlog-redispatch-sweep.ts`, migration 084).** Mirrors the existing `QC_MAX_REROUTES` pattern: a task stuck in the cheap re-dispatch loop (config problem or an unresolved hold that never reaches `recordDispatchFailure`) is now escalated to `status='blocked'` once it has both exceeded `REDISPATCH_MAX_ATTEMPTS` (K=20, env-overridable) retries AND been stuck for at least `REDISPATCH_ESCALATE_HOURS` (M=6h, env-overridable) — closing the last permanent-reloop path. New `tasks.redispatch_count` column (migration 084, idempotent `ALTER TABLE`) tracks the cheap-retry count per task. Escalation writes a `[REDISPATCH-CAP]` note with `block_audience='SYSTEM'` (operator feed only — no client Telegram, per the silent-updates doctrine) so a config-level stall reaches the operator, not the client. `tests/unit/point6-backlog-redispatch-cap.test.ts` covers the K-and-M cap logic and the SYSTEM-audience block note.
- **Migrations 083 / 084** are sequential (latest before this was 082), idempotent (`PRAGMA table_info` guard before `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN`), additive, and run on boot. No schema regression to any already-shipped column.
- No client names in any changed file. Box user, not root.

## [v4.58.0] — 2026-07-01 — fix(release-hygiene): repair-script self-heal restored, no-client-names/shell-syntax CI gates, committed roster purge, platform-safe dispatch fallback, sync-departments canonical-path resolution, model-sovereignty parity, status-route auth hardening, migration-058 index fix, vitest/node:test glob fix

Consolidates a batch of release-hygiene and hardening fixes surfaced during the repo review sprint. All additive/idempotent; no client names in any changed file (repo is fleet-wide); box user, not root.

- **`scripts/repair-command-center.sh` syntax fix — self-heal un-killed.** A shell syntax error was short-circuiting the self-heal before it reached step (a), the `better-sqlite3` native-module ABI rebuild (`npm rebuild better-sqlite3`, followed by a load-and-query smoke check confirming the module's compiled ABI matches the running Node ABI). `bash -n scripts/repair-command-center.sh` now parses clean and the self-heal runs end-to-end again.
- **Tracked-file client-data gate — `scripts/qc-assert-no-client-names.sh` v1.1.0.** Adds a NUMERIC client Telegram chat-ID denylist class (PRD P0-3 follow-up) alongside the existing name/keyword scan, with a masked-output convention so a caught offender's value is never echoed in full to CI logs. This closes the gap in `qc-blocked-gate.sh` Assertion 5, which only scans the git diff and never catches a client name that was already committed — this gate walks every tracked file on disk instead.
- **New CI jobs (`.github/workflows/qc-cc.yml`).** **`no-client-names`** — runs a hermetic self-test (a planted client-name fixture must fail the gate) before running the authoritative tracked-file scan against the real repo. **`shell-syntax`** — runs `bash -n` over every tracked `*.sh` file (root `scripts/`, `scripts/install/`, `scripts/cloudflare/`, `scripts/integration-tests/`, `scripts/conversational-ai/`, `fleet-heartbeat/scripts/`, `.claude/`) so a broken heredoc or quoting error can never ship again — the same class of bug this release's repair-script fix corrected.
- **Committed client/operator data purged.** The fleet roster (client box labels, IPs, container names, SSH aliases) is no longer tracked in this fleet-wide repo. `fleet-heartbeat/scripts/propagate-rescue-webhook.sh` now loads it at runtime from operator-local files (`RESCUE_VPS_ROSTER_FILE` / `RESCUE_MAC_ROSTER_FILE`, defaulting under the operator's own accounts directory), warning loudly instead of silently no-op'ing when a roster file is absent or empty.
- **Dispatch runtime — platform detection replaces the hardcoded home fallback (`src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts`, P1-5).** The specialist-runtime path resolver no longer falls back to a hardcoded operator home directory; it now resolves via `process.env.HOME || process.env.USERPROFILE || os.homedir()` so a box where `HOME` is unset (PM2/systemd/container contexts) still resolves correctly. New no-literal test `tests/unit/p1-5-no-hardcoded-operator-home.test.ts` asserts the source contains no hardcoded absolute home path.
- **`scripts/sync-departments-from-build-state.py` canonical-path resolution.** Now resolves the canonical master-files roots, the VPS DB path, and `companySlug` correctly instead of assuming a single fixed layout, so the sync succeeds across Mac-mini and VPS installs alike. 11 new pytest cases cover the resolution paths.
- **Model sovereignty.** `FORBIDDEN_PREFIXES` (`src/lib/model-selector.ts`) is kept at full parity with the onboarding Python selector's forbidden-prefix list. The Anthropic connector (`src/lib/model-providers/index.ts`) is gated behind `ALLOW_ANTHROPIC_PROVIDER` (default OFF) so it is never available to selection on a client box unless an operator explicitly opts in. A demo-seed fixture's slug that referenced a specific value was swapped for a generic placeholder.
- **Status route auth hardening (`src/app/api/tasks/[id]/status/route.ts`).** The `WEBHOOK_SECRET` HMAC middleware gate now covers this dynamic route the same way it already covers `/api/tasks/ingest`. `'done'` is rejected with 403 unconditionally, regardless of auth. `'blocked'` is scoped: a signed caller may only move a card into `blocked` when it is Skill-6-marked, closing the gap where any signed caller could force-block an arbitrary card. 9 new pinning tests cover the auth/scope matrix.
- **Migration 058 — `idx_tasks_archived_at` index now created unconditionally.** The `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` was previously nested inside the column-absence guard, so a fresh install (where `schema.ts` already declares `archived_at`) skipped the `ALTER TABLE` branch and never got the index. The index create now runs outside that guard on every DB, old or new — idempotent either way.
- **`vitest.config.ts` / Node `:test` glob collision fixed.** `vitest run` no longer picks up test files intended for the Node built-in test runner (`npm run test:unit` via `tsx --test`), eliminating spurious "no test suite found" failures between the two suites.
- No migration schema regression to any already-shipped column. No client names in any changed file.

## [v4.57.0] — 2026-07-01 — feat: task status-transition consumer endpoint (Skill-6 Kanban)

- **New consumer endpoint `POST /api/tasks/[id]/status` (`src/app/api/tasks/[id]/status/route.ts`).** Applies a board task's status transition delivered by the `cc_board.py` producer. Authenticates via `Authorization: Bearer <MC_API_TOKEN>` and verifies `x-webhook-signature` = HMAC-SHA256(raw body, `WEBHOOK_SECRET`) as lowercase hex — both constant-time. On a valid transition it mutates the task status, emits a `task_status_changed` event, and writes a `task_history` row; rejects bad signature/token (401), unknown id (404), invalid status (400).
- **Verified end-to-end** against the already-committed `cc_board.py` producer: producer HMAC equals consumer HMAC over identical raw bytes; a tampered body is rejected (401) while the untampered control passes (200). Unit suite `tests/unit/task-status-transition.test.ts` (5/5) + `tsc --noEmit` clean.
- No migration, no schema change. Additive. No client names in changed files.

## [v4.56.2] — 2026-06-29 — fix: FM-6 dedupe welcome task rows + correct presentations model_id env-default path

- **FM-6 dedupe fix — `src/app/api/departments/route.ts`:** `createDepartmentInDbDirect` had no idempotency on the "Welcome to …" starter-task INSERT. Every call that bypassed the outer workspace-exists check (parallel requests, external scripts, aborted transactions) could insert a second row with the same title and workspace_id. Added a check-before-insert guard inside the transaction: `SELECT id FROM tasks WHERE workspace_id = ? AND title = ? LIMIT 1` — if a row already exists, its id is reused and the INSERT is skipped. Minimal, schema-free, consistent with the codebase's existing check-before-insert pattern.
- **FM-6c env-default gap fix — `src/lib/model-selector.ts`:** `resolveSovereignDefault()` checked `checkModelSovereignty()` for the `SOVEREIGN_DEFAULT_MODEL` env var, but that function skips the modality check when `required_modality === 'text'` (it only validates wrong-modality for non-text tasks). A TTS model set as the env default therefore passed sovereignty and was returned as the reasoning `model_id` for any text task — including presentations tasks. Added the same `canServeTextTask()` guard used by the eligible-inventory scan: if `required_modality === 'text'` and the env-default model is a pure TTS/media model, the env default is skipped and the inventory scan runs. No change to behavior for non-text modalities or for language-model env defaults.
- No migration, no schema change. No client names in changed files. Additive + idempotent.

## [v4.56.1] — 2026-06-29 — feat: Presentations board-resilience completion — FIX C v2 (matching cert), SOP-furnace reaper, model_id TTS fix, dispatcher canonical-runtime, department dedup (FM-6)

Completes the Command-Center half of the Presentation-department remediation, building ON v4.56.0 (#118, which shipped the ingest self-heal + the v1 presence-only done-gate). This release does NOT regress #118: its FIX J (`ingest/route.ts` schema self-heal + 503 + `notifyOwnerSchemaError`) and `validation.ts` field are kept as-is; the done-gate enforcement is preserved and STRENGTHENED. All items additive + idempotent; no client names in any changed file (repo is fleet-wide); box user, not root. The [ALREADY SHIPPED] pieces (`tasks.sop_id` + migration 056 + backfill 053; `resolveWorkspaceId` no-bare-`default`; `isWorkforceProvisioned` gate) were re-verified present and left UNCHANGED.

- **FIX C v2 — deck no-skip proof now MATCHED, not just present (`src/app/api/tasks/[id]/route.ts`, `src/lib/presentations-cert-gate.ts`, migration 080).** v4.56.0 enforced a non-empty `process_certificate_sha` and explicitly deferred "verification against a stored certificate hash" to v2 — this delivers it. New `tasks.process_certificate_sha` column (migration 080, additive/nullable) stores the registered cert. The pure, unit-tested `evaluatePresentationsDoneGate()` decides: none stored + none presented → reject (still required, no regression); a registered cert → the mover MUST present the SAME sha (anti-spoof) else reject; a valid sha presented with none stored → accept + persist as the certificate of record. Rejections keep v4.56.0's `422` + `requires_process_certificate` response shape (now also carrying `code` + `remediation`). Scoped to `presentations`; other departments unaffected.
- **FM-6b — SOP-authoring furnace stopped (`src/lib/sop-authoring.ts`, `src/lib/db/task-dedup.ts`, migration 082).** The dispatch sweep re-created an identical open `Author SOP: …` sub-task every ~2 min (hundreds stuck `in_progress`). A runtime IDEMPOTENCY GUARD reuses an existing open authoring sub-task (matched on the original-task link OR title+department) and returns a new `deduped` status instead of inserting another; migration 082 + the exported `reapDuplicateOpenAuthoringTasks()` FK-safely collapse pre-existing clones (keep the oldest). The existing W8.2 attempt cap already hard-stops `no_specialist_runtime` redispatch after `MAX_DISPATCH_ATTEMPTS`.
- **FM-6c — model_id no longer populated from the wrong field (`src/lib/model-selector.ts`).** A pure media/TTS model (e.g. `gpt-4o-mini-tts`, capability `audio_generation` only) could win a TEXT task because the modality filter accepted ANY model for `text`. A new `canServeTextTask()` predicate excludes pure media-output/embeddings models from text selection in BOTH `selectTaskModel()` and the `resolveSovereignDefault()` Layer-4b fallback, so a presentations/text task can never pin a TTS model as its reasoning `model_id`.
- **Dispatcher legacy-slug → runtime (`src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts`).** `resolveSpecialistSessionKey()` now probes the CANONICAL runtime dir (`canonicalDeptSlug`) for an aliased workspace slug (`ceo` → `dept-master-orchestrator`, `app-development` → `engineering`) before reporting `no_specialist_runtime`, so an aliased department DISPATCHES instead of looping in backoff. Dispatch is NOT gated on a NULL `agents.model` — the resolver's sovereign-default + the W8.2 cap already fall back to the box's configured model or surface ONE clear wiring error (re-verified; no infinite refuse-loop).
- **Department single-source / dedup (`src/lib/db/task-dedup.ts`, migration 081, seeding-path guards).** Duplicate workspace rows that canonicalize to ONE department (`ceo` + `master-orchestrator`, `app-development` + `engineering`) are merged to the canonical keeper (`dedupeCanonicalWorkspaces`, migration 081), reassigning every `workspace_id`-bearing row before deleting the loser. Direction follows the repo's single source of truth `canonicalDeptSlug()` (the 2026-06-28 UNIT-ENG promotion made `engineering` canonical) so the board's list stays consistent with routing — merging the other way would orphan routed tasks. A slug-uniqueness guard (`findCanonicalWorkspaceId`) at every seeding path (`autoSeedFromDepartmentsJson`, `reseedWorkspacesFromConfig`, the `createDepartmentInDbDirect` operator override) prevents re-creating a second row for an existing department.
- **Migrations 080 / 081 / 082** are sequential (latest before this was 079; #118 added none), idempotent, and run on boot. **No schema regression** to any [ALREADY SHIPPED] column.
- **Guards/tests (`tests/unit/`, Node test runner, isolated throwaway DBs):** `presentations-cert-gate` (done-gate requires + anti-spoofs the cert), `model-selector-text-serviceability` (TTS never selected for text; NULL-model sovereign-default still resolves), `cc-board-dedup-reaper` (no duplicate department slugs; reaper idempotent — no duplicate open tasks; legacy slug → canonical runtime; migration-080 column present), `sop-authoring-idempotency` (open authoring sub-task reused, none re-created).
- **Independent verification:** `tsc --noEmit`, `scripts/qc-cc.sh` (111 green), and `npm run build` pass; every existing unit suite in the touched areas (model-sovereignty, fast-loop-QC, owner-notify, trio-seed, workspace-FK, ingest-dedup, routing) passes in isolation; a stash-to-`main` baseline confirmed the bulk-run flakiness set is pre-existing and unchanged by this PR.

## [v4.56.0]  —  2026-06-29  —  feat(resilience+presentations): ingest schema-error self-heal + owner escalation; presentations done-gate (no-skip proof at the board)

Two additive, low-risk hardening items for the task capture pipeline and the presentations department gate.

**EDIT 1 — Ingest catch block: schema-error self-heal + clear 503 + owner escalation (`src/app/api/tasks/ingest/route.ts`)**

The existing catch block returned a blind `500 Internal server error` with no distinction between a generic crash and a schema problem. The canonical failure mode is a box whose migrations have not yet run or ran partially (e.g. `SQLITE_ERROR: table tasks has no column named sop_id` — the historical migration 056 case, or `stage_slug` for 079). The new block:

- Detects schema errors via `/SqliteError|no column named|no such column|no such table/i`.
- Attempts a one-shot self-heal: `runMigrations(getDb())` runs pending migrations in-process so future requests succeed (best-effort, own try/catch).
- Escalates: calls `notifyOwnerSchemaError(msg)` (best-effort, gateway-routed via `notifyOwner`) so the owner is told the box needs `npm run db:seed` / a redeploy.
- Returns a CLEAR 503 with `{ error, detail, remediation, schema_error: true }` instead of an opaque 500. The caller can distinguish a schema problem and retry.
- BUILD-SAFE: task-field variables (`title`, `finalDescription`, etc.) are declared inside the try block and are NOT in scope in the catch — no `createTaskCore` retry is attempted. The self-heal brings the schema current for the next request; the caller must retry.
- Non-schema failures still return a 500 with `detail: msg` added.

New imports: `getDb` added to the existing `@/lib/db` import; `runMigrations` from `@/lib/db/migrations`; `notifyOwnerSchemaError` added to the existing `@/lib/owner-reports` import.

**EDIT 1b — `notifyOwnerSchemaError` (`src/lib/owner-reports.ts`)**

New export, modeled on `notifyOwnerAssigned`. Gateway-routed via `notifyOwner`; fail-soft; returns boolean; never throws into the request path.

**Presentations done-gate — `process_certificate_sha` required at the board (`src/app/api/tasks/[id]/route.ts`, `src/lib/validation.ts`)**

Any PATCH that transitions a task whose department canonical-slug is `presentations` to `status: 'done'` now REQUIRES a non-empty `process_certificate_sha` in the request body. If missing or empty the endpoint rejects with 422 `{ error: '...', requires_process_certificate: true }` before the status commit — the board cannot be marked done without proof the no-skip floor script ran. Other departments are completely unaffected (slug check is scoped to `presentations` only; the gate is inside the existing status-transition block after the Triad gate and before `updates.push('status = ?')`).

`UpdateTaskSchema` in `src/lib/validation.ts` gains an optional `process_certificate_sha: z.string().optional()` field so the Zod parse accepts the field from the body; the API route enforces presence for presentations specifically.

v1 note: presence of the hash is the gate; verification of the hash value against a stored certificate is a planned v2 addition. This ships the board-side enforcement that prevents any path — agent or human drag — from closing a presentations task without the prove-deck.py proof token.

- No migration, no schema column change. No client names. Box user, not root.
- **PROOF** — `npm run build` (next build / typecheck) green; `npx vitest run` green. No client names in changed files.

## [v4.55.4] — 2026-06-29 — fix(pm2): reconcile the WHOLE repo to the fleet-canonical app name `blackceo-command-center` (supersedes v4.55.3's interim direction)

The fleet-canonical pm2 app name is **`blackceo-command-center`** — the name the openclaw-onboarding installer, every per-box fleet dedup, and `scripts/deploy.sh` standardize on. Earlier revisions of THIS repo diverged to `mission-control` across `ecosystem.config.cjs`, the `scripts/install/*-bootstrap.sh` ecosystem templates, `scripts/deploy.sh`, and `scripts/watchdog-cc.sh` self-heal. On a box already running `blackceo-command-center`, that divergence meant `pm2 resurrect` / a bootstrap re-run / a watchdog self-heal would (re)create a SECOND app named `mission-control` on :4000 — the two-process mutual-kill loop that wedged a client box. (v4.55.3 documented the contract but pointed the comment at the wrong name; this release corrects every file.)

- **`ecosystem.config.cjs`** — `name` is now `blackceo-command-center` (was `mission-control`). This is what `pm2 resurrect` restores at boot and what `pm2 start ecosystem.config.cjs` (watchdog self-heal, INSTALL guidance) creates, so it can no longer spawn a rival. The on-disk `DATABASE_PATH` filename stays `mission-control.db` — that is a file path, NOT the app name.
- **`scripts/install/mac-mini-bootstrap.sh` + `scripts/install/vps-docker-bootstrap.sh`** — the written ecosystem template `name` is now `blackceo-command-center`, and the idempotent-heal reconcile now treats a stale `"mission-control"` (and the older bare `"command-center"`) as needing-update, so a re-bootstrap converges an old box to the canonical name.
- **`scripts/deploy.sh`** — `PM2_NAME="blackceo-command-center"`.
- **`scripts/watchdog-cc.sh`** — self-heal still clears EVERY CC app name (canonical + legacy) and restarts via `pm2 start ecosystem.config.cjs`; because ecosystem now declares `blackceo-command-center`, the end state is always exactly one canonical CC and the legacy `mission-control` is never resurrected. Misleading "legacy" comments corrected.
- **`scripts/cc-start.sh`** — the v4.55.3 orphan-port-killer self-pid safety (`$$`/`$PPID` exclusion) is retained; its comment now names the correct canonical.
- **Docs** — `DEPLOYMENT.md` and `docs/OPENCLAW_BRIDGE_PAIRING.md` pm2 command references reconciled to `blackceo-command-center` (DB-file / install-dir references left as-is).
- **PROOF** — drove the REAL `scripts/watchdog-cc.sh` self-heal + `pm2 start ecosystem.config.cjs` against a box already running `blackceo-command-center`: a zombie `{blackceo-command-center, mission-control}` converges to exactly one `blackceo-command-center` (mission-control retired, never resurrected); a healthy box is untouched; the ecosystem start spawns no duplicate.
- Note: `package.json` `name` ("mission-control") is the npm package identity, NOT a pm2 app name, and is intentionally left unchanged to avoid package-lock / npm-ci churn. No migration, no schema change, no config/template change. Box user, not root. No client names in changed files.

## [v4.55.3] — 2026-06-29 — fix(pm2): document the fleet-canonical app name + harden cc-start.sh orphan-port killer against self/supervisor kills (two-CC-on-:4000 defence-in-depth)

- **Context — the root cause (fixed in the onboarding installer, hardened here).** A box could end up running the Command Center under TWO pm2 app names at once: `mission-control` (what `ecosystem.config.cjs`, `pm2 resurrect`, `scripts/watchdog-cc.sh`, and the `scripts/install/*-bootstrap.sh` scripts all use) and the divergent `blackceo-command-center` that the openclaw-onboarding installer historically started — with BOTH bound to :4000. The two `next start` children then mutually killed each other through cc-start.sh's orphan-port killer: an endless restart loop (47k+ restarts) that wedged the gateway on a client box. The app-name unification lands in the installer (openclaw-onboarding v16.1.6, Phase 6 reconcile + start-from-ecosystem); this release closes the two remaining CC-repo gaps.
- **`ecosystem.config.cjs` — canonical-name contract documented in-code.** Added a comment above `name: 'mission-control'` declaring it the SINGLE fleet-canonical pm2 app name and listing every tool that must agree (this config, watchdog-cc.sh, the bootstrap scripts, package.json, the installer Phase 6). The value is unchanged — `mission-control` was already canonical — so there is no behavioural change and the port-pin / circuit-breaker guards (qc-cc.sh §11.1–§11.9) still hold.
- **`scripts/cc-start.sh` — orphan-port killer self-pid safety.** `free_port()` now strips this launcher's own pid (`$$`) and its pm2/npm supervisor (`$PPID`) from the kill list via a new `_cc_strip_protected` helper, applied to the initial port scan, the post-TERM re-probe, and the final check. With one canonical pm2 app there is no longer a sibling CC to fight, so the killer can no longer cause the mutual-kill; the pid exclusion is defence-in-depth so cc-start.sh can never SIGTERM the process tree that supervises the canonical CC. Any LISTENer remaining after the exclusion is, by definition, a stale orphan from a prior boot/restart and is still safely reclaimed. The env-bleed strip (`unset PORT`, qc-cc.sh §11.4) and the lsof/fuser orphan detection (§11.5) are unchanged.
- No migration, no schema change, no config/template change. Box user, not root. No client names in changed files.

## [v4.55.2] — 2026-06-28 — fix(db): self-heal `tasks.stage_slug` (migration-ID-074 collision) so ad-campaign card-create stops 500ing

- Migration 079 (`ensure_tasks_stage_slug`, idempotent `PRAGMA table_info` guard + `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` ×2): `ALTER TABLE tasks ADD COLUMN stage_slug TEXT` plus the two ad-campaign indexes. Mirrors migration 074's body exactly; additive + nullable, never touches existing rows or routes.
- **Root cause:** the migration runner keys applied-state on `id` alone (`_migrations.id`). An earlier source revision numbered a since-removed migration as id `074`; current source assigns id `074` to `add_tasks_stage_slug_for_ad_campaigns`. Any DB that recorded the OLD `074` silently SKIPS the current `074` forever, so `tasks.stage_slug` is never created on those DBs.
- **Symptom (same class as migration 056 `sop_id` and 078 `block_reason`):** the ad-campaign assembly-line INSERT in `src/lib/ad-campaigns.ts` writes `stage_slug`, so on an affected DB it throws `SQLITE_ERROR: table tasks has no column named stage_slug` and the ad-run card-create path returns HTTP 500. Reproduced and verified against a live DB carrying the `074` collision.
- A NEW migration id (`079`) is used so it always runs on affected DBs; idempotent so it is a no-op where `074` already added the column. `schema.ts` already declares `stage_slug` in the base `CREATE TABLE tasks`, so fresh installs were never affected.
- **Audit note:** the canonical task ingest/create path (`createTaskCore`, used by `POST /api/tasks` and `POST /api/tasks/ingest`) writes `sop_id`, which is already covered by migration 056 + `schema.ts`; a full column-drift audit confirmed `stage_slug` was the only code-written `tasks` column missing on a live DB.

## [v4.55.1] — 2026-06-28 — fix(W8): add block_reason column so gateway-down/stuck tasks actually transition to blocked + notify owner

- Migration 078 (idempotent `PRAGMA table_info` guard): `ALTER TABLE tasks ADD COLUMN block_reason TEXT`.
- Without this column the block-on-N UPDATE in `recordDispatchFailure` (task-dispatcher.ts) and the QC-BLOCKED UPDATE in `qc-scorer.ts` threw SQLITE_ERROR "no such column: block_reason"; the throw was caught and swallowed, leaving tasks stuck in backoff forever and owner notifications never firing.
- After this migration: a task reaching `MAX_DISPATCH_ATTEMPTS` correctly transitions to `status='blocked'`, increments `dispatch_attempts` to the cap, sets `next_dispatch_eligible_at = NULL`, and fires `notifyOwner`. The re-loop-on-backoff path is structurally eliminated.
- Removed stale `.bak` siblings under `src/lib/` and `src/app/api/`.

## [v4.55.0] — 2026-06-28 — feat: W8 board-liveness + furnace-safe guards, W4 full-context handoff, W5 owner notifications, W3 routing gate + general fallback + owner-direct

Ships the four Work items that close the "nothing sticks" board-liveness failure:
**W8** (board-liveness + furnace-safe advancement), **W4** (full-context handoff), **W5** (owner notifications), and **W3** (routing gate + general fallback + owner-direct specialist pin).

**W8 — Board-liveness + furnace-safe guards (migration 077, new job, model-selector, sweeps):**
- Migration 077 adds `dispatch_attempts`, `last_dispatch_attempt_at`, `next_dispatch_eligible_at` columns to `tasks` (idempotent `ALTER TABLE` + partial index). Enables per-task backoff accounting without touching any existing row.
- `src/lib/jobs/intake-advance-sweep.ts` (new): THE single board-advancement authority. Every 2 min it drains every intake lane (`inbox`/`backlog`/`planning`/`pending_dispatch`/`assigned`): routes unassigned tasks, feeds campaign boards (W8.4), and fires `autoDispatchTask`. Furnace-proof by construction: selects only tasks under the QC re-route cap, under the dispatch-attempt cap, and past their exponential-backoff window — so an unadvanceable task drops out instead of being re-fired forever. Registered in scheduler JOBS[] as `intake-advance`. Disable with `INTAKE_ADVANCE_SWEEP_ENABLED=0`.
- `src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts`: `recordDispatchFailure()` + `recordDispatchSuccess()` helpers stamp attempt-accounting on every failed/successful advance, backing off exponentially (default 120 s base, 2× per attempt, cap 3600 s). After `MAX_DISPATCH_ATTEMPTS` (default 5) the task is hard-blocked (visible on board) and the owner is notified — silent re-looping is structurally impossible. Guard 6 (backoff window check) added to `autoDispatchTask` so even mid-tick re-selections are cheap no-ops.
- `src/lib/model-selector.ts`: `resolveSovereignDefault()` (new) guarantees a non-null, sovereign, modality-fit model as the dispatch last resort, eliminating the 172/183 null-`model_id` root cause. Respects `SOVEREIGN_DEFAULT_MODEL` env, then walks the client's inventory tier 1→2→3. Never substitutes an owner's express model.
- `src/lib/jobs/backlog-redispatch-sweep.ts` + `src/lib/jobs/ceo-delegation-sweep.ts`: Both sweeps now honour the `dispatch_attempts` cap and `next_dispatch_eligible_at` backoff window in their SELECT query — a blocked or backed-off task cannot re-enter the fire queue from either sweep either. Both sweeps remain PAUSED (`*_ENABLED=0`) pending `intake-advance` verification.
- `src/lib/campaigns.ts` (new): `ensureCampaignForTask()` — creates or attaches a task to its department's live campaign board (W8.4). Called by `intake-advance-sweep`.

**W4 — Full-context handoff (`src/lib/context-pack.ts` new, `src/lib/task-dispatcher.ts`):**
- `src/lib/context-pack.ts` (new): Assembles a typed `ContextPack` for every dispatched task. Includes task-targeted excerpts of the receiving specialist's core files (`AGENTS.md`/`TOOLS.md`/`MEMORY.md`), pointer references to `how-to-use-this-department.md`, OpenClaw master files, the SOP, and per-domain research sources. Also threads optional `context_refs` from the ingest payload (W4.1) so the CEO can pass explicit doc pointers.
- `autoDispatchTask` splices the rendered context pack into the task message before dispatch — the receiving specialist never starts blind.

**W5 — Owner notifications (`src/lib/owner-reports.ts` new, dispatcher + ingest):**
- `src/lib/owner-reports.ts` (new): Thin funnel for the three owner messages spec §5 requires: `notifyOwnerAssigned` ("I'm sending this to [Dept]"), `notifyOwnerStarted` (persona + dept + specialist + SOP + role), `notifyOwnerDone` (who + where-to-find-it). Each helper self-resolves all fields from the live DB given only a `taskId`. `notifyOwnerHeld` covers the held-task edge case.
- `notifyOwnerAssigned` called from `/api/tasks/ingest` on every successful routing result.
- `notifyOwnerStarted` called from `autoDispatchTask` immediately after dispatch write.
- `recordDispatchFailure` calls `notifyOwner` when a task hits the block cap.

**W3 — Routing gate + general fallback + owner-direct specialist pin:**
- `/api/tasks/ingest`: `isWorkforceProvisioned()` gate (W3.1) — routing applies only to boxes with a completed Zero Human Company interview AND materialized non-shell departments (spec §3). Shell/legacy boxes are exempt; tasks are still captured but not forced through department classification. Fail-safe: when the self-client row is absent, the gate defers to the materialized-departments signal alone.
- `WEBHOOK_SECRET` now required in production (W3.5): ingest returns 503 when unset in `NODE_ENV=production` instead of silently accepting unauthenticated writes.
- `src/lib/routing/department-router.ts`: `resolveSpecialistPin()` (new, W3.2) — owner-named specialist bypass. When the owner names a specific AI, the CEO routes STRAIGHT to it (id → exact name → exact persona → unique substring), bypassing `pickBestAgent` and department classification entirely. Falls through to normal routing when the named agent is not found. Wired as Step 0 in `comDispatch`.
- Ingest payload extended: `target_agent` / `specialist` accepted as specialist-pin aliases; `context_refs` for doc-pointer references.
- `src/lib/routing/canonical-slug.ts`: General fallback slug added — tasks with no resolvable department now fall into the `general-task` workspace rather than being dropped.

**NOTE: The furnace flags (`BACKLOG_REDISPATCH_SWEEP_ENABLED`, `CEO_DELEGATION_SWEEP_ENABLED`) REMAIN set to 0. Re-enable is a separate verified step once the `intake-advance` worker is confirmed draining the board.**

**Migrations note:** Migration 077 is idempotent (`PRAGMA table_info` guards on each `ALTER TABLE`; `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS`). Safe to apply to the live mission-control.db via a controlled `npm run db:migrate` — no destructive SQL. The live DB was NOT touched during this PR.

## [v4.53.2] — 2026-06-27 — fix: verified low-severity hygiene (FilePreview useEffect, chart guards, dead imports, LIKE escaping, any-types)

Applies five verified low-severity hygiene fixes. Two CRITICALs flagged in the QC report (auth-dead, SQL-injection) were independently verified as FALSE POSITIVES and intentionally NOT applied. ALLOW_INSECURE_OPEN_API was NOT set.

**Lane A — operator/FilePreview.tsx:** Replaced bare render-phase `fetchContent()` call with a `useEffect(() => { void fetchContent(); }, [src])` to comply with React's rules-of-hooks and stop the double-fetch on re-render.

**Lane B — ceo-board:**
- `ComparisonBar.tsx`: Added zero-division guards for `industryValue === 0` and `bestValue === 0` so the delta/percent calculations return 0 instead of NaN/Infinity on empty data.

**Lane C — lib:**
- `tasks.ts`: Escaped LIKE metacharacters (`%`, `_`, `\`) in the idempotency_key dedup query, using SQLite's `ESCAPE '\\'` clause, so keys containing those characters cannot false-match unrelated events.
- `openclaw/client.ts`: Replaced `any` parameter type on `generateEventId()` with a typed `GatewayFrame` interface covering only the fields the function reads.
- `routing/departments.config.ts`: Replaced two `any`-typed `db` parameters with `Database.Database` from `better-sqlite3`, removing the suppression comments.

## [v4.53.1] — 2026-06-27 — fix(fleet-heartbeat): jq/recreate-order bug in propagate-rescue-webhook.sh VPS secret block

Adds `fleet-heartbeat/scripts/propagate-rescue-webhook.sh` to origin/main for the first time and ships the jq/recreate-order bug fix flagged as a HANDOFF residual after the 2026-06-26 Rescue Rangers full-fleet propagation run.

**The bug (before):** In the VPS box loop the secret block (`RESCUE_RANGERS_WEBHOOK_SECRET` propagation) ran AFTER the `force-recreate` decision point. On any run where the webhook URL was already correct but the secret was new, `HOST_CHANGED` would be set to 1 AFTER the force-recreate check had already fired -- so the container was (re)created without the secret env var. The secret landed in the host `.env` file but the running container would not pick it up until the next manually triggered recreate.

**The fix (after):** The secret block now runs BEFORE the `force-recreate` check so `HOST_CHANGED` accumulates both the URL and secret deltas. A single `docker compose up -d --force-recreate` fires at the end and picks up both from the host `.env`.

**Additional fixes in the same file:**
- jq quoting hardened: replaced `docker exec sh -c "..."` (double-quoted body where shell expands `$k`/`$v` before jq sees them) with `docker exec -u node -e SK=... -e SV=... sh -c '...'` (single-quoted body; variables passed as env vars named SK/SV, never touched by the shell before jq).
- Idempotent "already correct" guard added for the secret in host `.env` to suppress spurious `HOST_CHANGED` on re-runs.
- `make_section()` upgraded to v2 structured-form: takes `box_name` and `box_type` args and emits a 9-field escalation payload (`person`, `clientName`, `agentName`, `boxName`, `boxType`, `openclawVersion`, `problem`, `alreadyTried`, `returnTo`) instead of the flat one-liner. Old v1 sections are detected and replaced in-place.
- An opted-out client's entry commented out (opted out of fleet-heartbeat propagation).
- Verify block extended: now also prints the `RESCUE_RANGERS_WEBHOOK_SECRET` presence and the `X-Rescue-Secret` header count in AGENTS.md.

**Files changed:** `fleet-heartbeat/scripts/propagate-rescue-webhook.sh` (new on origin/main).

## [v4.53.0] — 2026-06-26 — fix(dispatch): dispatch/route.ts null-fallback + dept-prefix resolver for Skill-6 Kanban flow

Closes the last gap in the Skill-6 (funnel/website) → Kanban demo path. Two files edited; no other files touched.

**dispatch/route.ts — `resolveSpecialistSessionKey` null-fallback (FG1):**
The route handler's copy of `resolveSpecialistSessionKey` still returned `agent:main:<session>` when no specialist runtime was found, sending every manual "Send to Agent" click to the CEO/Stefanie orchestrator whose prompt forbids building — she re-ingests the task (loop). Return type changed from `string` to `string | null`. On Attempt-1 (workspace-slug) the function now probes `~/.openclaw/agents/dept-<slug>/` BEFORE `~/.openclaw/agents/<slug>/` so live boxes (whose runtime dirs are `dept-funnels` / `dept-web-development`, not bare slugs) resolve on the first probe. When no runtime resolves, returns `null` — the caller writes a durable `routed_but_not_dispatched` row to `task_activities` + `events`, leaves the task in `backlog` (visible on board), and returns HTTP 202 `{success:false, held:true}` instead of feeding the CEO loop. Matches the hardened null-return that `task-dispatcher.ts` already had (v4.52.0, G8).

**task-dispatcher.ts — Attempt-1 dept-prefix probe (FG1):**
Same dept-prefix-first probe added to the `autoDispatchTask` path for consistency. The null-fallback refusal was already correct; only the probe order was wrong (bare-slug-first missed `dept-funnels` / `dept-web-development`).

Proof harness (5/5 pass, cited below):
- T1: funnels workspace slug → `agent:dept-funnels:<session>`
- T2: web-development workspace slug → `agent:dept-web-development:<session>`
- T3: unknown dept → null (`routed_but_not_dispatched`, NOT `agent:main`)
- T4: funnels role slug → `agent:dept-funnels:<session>`
- T5: bare 'funnels' dir absent → fix correctly probes dept-prefix first

## [v4.52.0] — 2026-06-26 — feat(workforce-engine): kanban push-through wiring + persona/SOP resolve + auth hardening

Command-Center half of the end-to-end AI-workforce ENGINE hardening (companion to openclaw-onboarding v14.3.3). Additive and separate from the concurrent ad-campaigns (v4.50.0), column-tooltips, and CEO/board workflows. Fixes Trevor's core worry that cards "sit at the very beginning and never move/assign/progress," plus persona/SOP wiring and a fail-closed auth posture.

KANBAN PUSH-THROUGH (G8) — the dispatcher (`task-dispatcher.ts`) is the ONLY correct authority for the `backlog → in_progress` flip (it flips AFTER `chat.send` succeeds). Two callers were pre-setting `in_progress`, so `autoDispatchTask` returned at GUARD-3 and the agent was never invoked. `webhooks/auto-route/route.ts` and `jobs/ceo-delegation-sweep.ts` now assign agent/department and LEAVE the card in backlog for the dispatcher to flip. NEW `jobs/backlog-redispatch-sweep.ts` (registered `*/2` in `jobs/scheduler.ts`) re-fires assigned-but-stuck backlog cards — self-limiting at the root (grace window, batch cap, attempt cap, master/CEO exclusion, kill switch; a card drops out the instant it flips to in_progress; the failing path returns before any `chat.send`/LLM call → no token burn, no self-resurrect).

STATUS ENUM LOCKSTEP (G9/G14) — `validation.ts` shared `TaskStatus` enum widened 5→10 to the canonical board manifest (`inbox/planning/assigned/testing/pending_dispatch` added), so legitimate moves (e.g. the To-Do drop `status='assigned'`) and `inbox`-on-create stop returning 400. `task-lifecycle.ts` `LifecycleState`/`LEGAL_TRANSITIONS` extended to all 10 (strictly more permissive; no previously-legal edge removed) and the over-claimed docstring corrected to reality (transition() is advisory, not the sole gate). LOCKSTEP RECONCILE: ad-campaign stage cards now validate against a dedicated 5-value `AdCardStatus` enum instead of the widened `TaskStatus`, keeping the schema in lockstep with `moveAdStage()` (prevents a board-only status reaching an ad card). DB↔ENUM LOCKSTEP (Migration 076 `widen_tasks_status_check_to_10_board_statuses`): the runtime `tasks.status` CHECK constraint (schema.ts) only permitted the original 5 statuses, so every write of a new status (`assigned/inbox/planning/pending_dispatch/testing`) threw `SQLITE_CONSTRAINT` at runtime even though `tsc` was clean — cards literally could not leave backlog. Migration 076 runs SQLite's official 12-step table rebuild (reads the live CREATE TABLE sql, replaces only the CHECK, dynamic column copy, `foreign_key_check` gate, `useOuterTransaction:false`) to widen the CHECK to all 10 statuses; idempotent (no-op if already widened), column-set-agnostic, all indexes/triggers preserved. Renumbered to `076` on rebase (upstream v4.51.0 claimed `075` for the renumbered `intelligent_model_selector`).

PERSONA/SOP RESOLVE (G10/G11) — `tasks.ts` resolves+pins the persona (`resolvePersonaAndPin`, bounded retry, no cron) BEFORE auto-dispatch reads `tasks.persona_id`, so the board persona == the runtime persona. `tasks/[id]/route.ts` auto-resolves a missing SOP/persona in-band before the Triad gate decides, so a human drag no longer 400-bounces when the pin merely hadn't landed. `intelligence-resolver.ts` Hop-10 sticky lookup now keys on `(department_id, task_category)` (ported `inferTaskCategory`, byte-verified vs the Python source) instead of department alone, killing the cross-category misroute. `task-dispatcher.ts` refuses the silent `agent:main` fallback (returns null) and emits a durable, queryable `routed_but_not_dispatched` hold instead of feeding the CEO re-ingest loop.

FLOOR SEED (G12) — `db/migrations.ts` + `role-library-import.ts` + `system/converge/route.ts` resolve departments.json / the departments tree from the active client company folder (`ZERO_HUMAN_COMPANY_DIR` / `BLACKCEO_COMMAND_CENTER_ROOT` / newest materialized ZHC company), so a freshly-built client seeds its OWN floor instead of a stale repo-committed default — with the historic workspace path preserved as a checked candidate + fallback (operator box not broken).

AUTH HARDEN (G15) — `middleware.ts` is now fail-closed: missing `MC_API_TOKEN` rejects external `/api/*` (503) and the two webhook routes require `WEBHOOK_SECRET`, instead of silently passing all traffic through; same-origin UI + CF-Access path preserved; reversible via the explicit `ALLOW_INSECURE_OPEN_API=true` bridge (loud startup error names the var). The health bypass is a SUBTREE match (`/api/health`, `/api/health/`, `/api/health/deep`, …) so Cloudflare/CI liveness probes stay reachable with no token set — the deep-health thin-probe must never be gated. The pipeline duck-e2e drives the board via unauthenticated server-to-server fetches and is not testing auth, so its test server alone sets the `ALLOW_INSECURE_OPEN_API` escape hatch (production never does).

STALE UI (G16) — the dead per-column '+' is wired to the working New-Task flow; Call Mode / Web Agent lose the misleading "Soon" badges (both routes are fully built).

Lockstep/CI: version rolled to v4.52.0 across all 4 markers (`scripts/bump-version.sh`); full-project `tsc --noEmit` = 0 errors. Rebased onto current main (3191a25c, v4.51.0). Operator must create annotated tag v4.52.0 at ship (version-consistency tag guard).

## [v4.51.0] — 2026-06-26 — fix(ci): full CI green — dup-072 migration, QC 5.2 self-match, duck-e2e AF-I14 trace

Repairs every red CI check on main (was: Duck pipeline e2e, QC Command Center, Port-pin and env-bleed guard) without weakening any guardrail.

Migration: the id `072` was registered twice — `blocked_fields_and_last_progress_at` and `intelligent_model_selector`. The runner builds its applied-set once before the loop, so on a FRESH DB the second `072` still passed the in-memory `applied.has()` guard, ran, and its `INSERT INTO _migrations(id,…)` hit the PRIMARY KEY → `UNIQUE constraint failed: _migrations.id`, crashing the duck-e2e seed before migration 074. In production whichever `072` ran first claimed the id, so the SECOND migration's schema change (`sops.model_pin` + backfills) never applied. Fix: renumbered the second `072` → `075` (next free id; current max was 074) so it actually applies on the next deploy. The up-migration is idempotent/guarded (`PRAGMA table_info` column guard before `ALTER TABLE … ADD COLUMN`; `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` lifted out of the column guard so the partial index is ensured whether or not `model_pin` pre-existed; `agent_settings`/`tasks.model_id` backfills are no-ops when empty) and additive/reversible — manual down documented in the migration body (`DROP INDEX IF EXISTS idx_sops_model_pin; ALTER TABLE sops DROP COLUMN model_pin; DELETE FROM _migrations WHERE id='075';`). Existing prod DBs are untouched: the first `072` keeps its recorded id; the renamed migration runs once as `075`. Array position (and thus execution order) is unchanged. No destructive drops/renames.

QC gate: check `5.2` ("no 'anthropic/' provider id in src/lib") was a false-positive — it flagged its OWN negative-list declaration `const FORBIDDEN_PREFIXES = ['anthropic/', …]` in `model-selector.ts` (the guard that BANS Anthropic). Refined `scripts/qc-cc.sh` check 5.2 to exclude lines containing `FORBIDDEN_PREFIXES` (mirrors the `grep -v` style of check 5.1); real usage (e.g. `model: 'anthropic/claude-…'`) carries no `FORBIDDEN_PREFIXES` on the line and is still caught. Because both the "QC Command Center" job and the "Port-pin and env-bleed guard" job run the full `qc-cc.sh`, this single fix turns BOTH jobs green (the port/env-bleed section 11 self-tests already passed — there was no real port defect). `qc-cc.sh` now: PASS — 108 checks green, 0 warnings.

Duck e2e (test-only, AF-I14 unchanged): with the seed crash gone, two previously-masked subtests (g/h) surfaced. The AF-I14 KIE.ai image-path guardrail (broadened fleet-wide at v4.45.0) fail-closes any task whose title describes an image deliverable ("create a blue duck image") unless it finds an OpenClaw session exec trace proving `scripts/kie_generate.py` was used; the mock generator ships a PNG with no such trace → VIOLATION-C → status `backlog` (escalation to `blocked` is cron-deferred and the cron doesn't run under `next start`). Fix is in the test harness only: `tests/e2e/duck-test.ts` points the server's `HOME` at a throwaway dir and seeds a faithful KIE.ai session `.jsonl` trace (contains the taskId, a `python3 scripts/kie_generate.py` call and `api.kie.ai`, and no native `image_generate` tool block / dead endpoint) — the same artefact a real KIE-mode run records. AF-I14 then PASSES, the artifact-mode QC scores the PNG, and the task reaches a terminal state (`review`). The guardrail itself is untouched (fail-closed-on-no-trace is deliberate). Duck e2e now: 20/20 subtests pass.

Edited: `src/lib/db/migrations.ts` (072→075 renumber + hardened idempotency + documented down), `scripts/qc-cc.sh` (check 5.2 exclusion), `tests/e2e/duck-test.ts` (isolated HOME + seeded AF-I14 KIE.ai trace). Verification: `npm run build` exit 0; `npm run test:vitest` 73/73; `bash scripts/qc-cc.sh` exit 0 (108 green); duck-e2e 20/20.

## [v4.50.0] — 2026-06-26 — feat(board): ad-campaign cards (Skill 48 → Kanban)

Lands an external Facebook/Instagram ad assembly line on the existing board as a campaign + one card per stage, driven by the producer's receipt id. New `POST /api/ad-campaigns` (create-only, idempotent on `job_id`) creates a `campaigns` row + an epic parent card + one card per stage in `backlog`. New `PATCH /api/ad-campaigns/[id]` moves one stage card and is the SEPARATE status-update path: every move routes through the canonical `transition()` engine with `operatorOverride:true` (ad cards carry no assigned agent) so the two human pause points land on `review` without the QC auto-scorer skipping them. `GET /api/ad-campaigns?job_id=` polls a run. Auth mirrors `/api/tasks/ingest`: global Bearer middleware + per-route `x-webhook-signature` HMAC (both no-op when env unset). Creation uses a direct INSERT (mirrors `/api/campaigns`) — NOT `createTaskCore` — so no `autoDispatchTask()` agent runs fire per card; the OpenClaw `agent_id` is provenance only and is never written to the `assigned_agent_id` FK. Status map: created=backlog, working=in_progress, both human pauses=review, failure=blocked, approved=done.

Migration 074 `add_tasks_stage_slug_for_ad_campaigns` (additive + reversible): adds the single net-new column `tasks.stage_slug` (nullable; non-ad tasks stay NULL) plus a partial unique index `idx_tasks_campaign_stage` (one card per campaign_id+stage_slug) and `idx_tasks_stage_slug`. `campaign_id` and the blocked columns already exist (migrations 017 / 072). No destructive drops/renames. Manual rollback documented in the migration body (the runner has no auto-down; the change is purely additive so leaving it in place is safe): `DROP INDEX idx_tasks_campaign_stage; DROP INDEX idx_tasks_stage_slug; ALTER TABLE tasks DROP COLUMN stage_slug; DELETE FROM _migrations WHERE id='074';`. New files: `src/lib/ad-campaigns.ts`, `src/app/api/ad-campaigns/route.ts`, `src/app/api/ad-campaigns/[id]/route.ts`, `tests/unit/ad-campaigns.test.ts`. Edited: `validation.ts` (two zod schemas), `db/schema.ts` (stage_slug column), `db/migrations.ts` (id 074).

## [v4.49.0] — 2026-06-16 — feat(qc): AF-COVERAGE anti-compression gate

Blocks a deck whose slide count is materially below what its source warrants (auto-fail) UNLESS a client_requested_slide_cap is on record. Closes the hole where a rich transcript (~2800 lines, warranting ~30-62 slides) got silently compressed to a 12-slide summary. Pure checkCoverage(): FAIL if actual < 90% of slide_count_target with no cap; FAIL if large source (>1500 lines) + target <20 with no cap; PASS at >=90% of target or when an explicit client cap is honored; fail-closed on unknown. Emitted for deck tasks. Tests: AF-COVERAGE 14/14; AF-PIPELINE/SPELL/NUM/LANG/I14 regressions pass; tsc clean.
